The Pitiful Thirty-Nine Tribes 69

Since the arrival in Beijing of Peng Chu, representative of the thirty-nine tribes people from the northwest border of Kham and Tibet, the term "thirty-nine tribes" has begun to appear in the newspapers. Yesterday, this reporter visited Mr. Peng at his residence to inquire about everything, and the following is a summary of the information:

The Terrain of the Thirty-Nine Tribes: The thirty-nine tribes are located in the central part of the Kham-Tibet-Xining region, covering an area of approximately 6,000 li. They are located in the east of Tibet, approximately 200 li from Lhasa, and are closely connected to Lei Wu of Xikang. Their terrain is the most level of all the routes from China to Tibet. The China-Tibet Railway takes the Xining route, which is relatively easy to build. The route from Xining to Lhasa must pass through the tribe, which is a region that the country must pay close attention to in terms of transportation.

A Brief History of the Thirty-Nine Tribes: The people of Kham and Tibet call the thirty-nine tribes "Suoba," and in general parlance they are also called "Qiongbo." The meaning of Suoba is similar to that of a border defense commander, referring to a high-ranking official sent by the Chinese emperor to inspect the border defenses. Qiongbo means a person born from a bird's egg. It is said that the ancestor of the tribe was born from a bird's egg, so the people of Kham and Tibet still call them this to this day. Later, the territory was divided into thirty-nine tribes, i.e., thirty-nine large chieftains, each governing dozens of small chieftains, all of whom held hereditary positions. Above the thirty-nine chieftains was a chief administrator, equivalent to the governor of the former Qing Dynasty. Mr. Peng is one of the important members of the chief administrator's office.

The Thirty-Nine Tribes Have Belonged to the Chinese Territory for a Long Time and Have Always Been Known for Their Loyalty. Therefore, the people of Kham and Tibet also call them "Jiadeng," which means Han commoners. The Qing Dynasty's rule was inconsistent. Initially, they were under the jurisdiction of the Governor of Sichuan, but later they were transferred to the jurisdiction of the Minister Resident in Tibet. It is said that the Qing Imperial Envoy residing in Tibet would not be safe in Tibet without the protection of the thirty-nine tribes. According to the old rules, the thirty-nine tribes had 500 guards stationed at the Imperial Envoy's office in rotation. Since Zhao Erfeng led troops into Tibet during the late Qing Dynasty, the thirty-nine tribes have been providing conscripted labor and supplies, which is incomparable to peacetime, and the duties of the chief administrator and officials have naturally become heavier. Mr. Peng Chu is an important member of the chief administrator's office. He is young, intelligent, brave, and willing to take responsibility. He is also talented in literature and economics, so he is particularly committed to the idea of serving China. After the defeat of the border army, he and other tribesmen strongly advocated resisting Tibet. However, they suffered defeat due to inferior equipment and were captured and had their noses cut off. Many colleagues in the tribe at that time were stabbed in the feet and had their noses cut off, such as Si, Che Liwengji, Yu Xiningbu, etc., all of whom were outstanding figures of their time. However, they have not been heard of in China to this day and have not been recognized by our government, which cannot but make people sigh with emotion.

The Soil and Resources of the Thirty-Nine Tribes: The tribe has many plains, and the soil and resources are superior to those of Kham and Tibet. In addition to rice, various grains and wheat are abundantly produced, and many areas have two harvests a year. Gold mines are particularly abundant, and animal husbandry is their main industry. Various medicinal materials are their most exported products.

The People and Customs of the Thirty-Nine Tribes: The entire tribe worships Buddhism and generally observes the precept of not killing. The meat consumed by the people is slaughtered by those who make a living in the slaughtering business in foreign countries. The people, except for the lamas, are all natives, so they all wear lama robes. The lamas mostly belong to the Red Sect, and the Yellow Sect is less common. There are more than 180 temples of all sizes, and the major temples are all headed by Hutuktu. The people offer extremely sincere respect to the lamas. The tribe's internal politics are controlled by the chieftains of each tribe. The people are naturally strong and martial, and their spirit of defending the country and supporting chivalry is admirable. Their strong support for the border army at the beginning of the Republic, with one falling and another following, is a testament to this.

Mr. Peng's Experience After Arriving in Beijing: After arriving in Beijing for several months without making any progress, Mr. Peng was introduced to Yu Youren, the president of the Control Yuan, by Nuona Hutuktu. Yu gladly received him, inquired about everything in detail, and checked his background. He learned that he was a native of the thirty-nine tribes and had made contributions to China, unlike those who lived on the border and took the opportunity to act as representatives to seek wealth and status. He told Mr. Peng in person that there seemed to be no reason why the thirty-nine tribes' request to establish an office should not be approved. He could submit another petition to the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission. Therefore, Mr. Peng continued to submit a petition, which read as follows: "Submitting a petition to earnestly request attention to the border areas and approval to establish an office so that our tribe can return to Chinese jurisdiction. Our thirty-nine tribes have belonged to Chinese territory for a long time. Since the Qing Dynasty, we have paid tribute to the country and worked diligently for the royal affairs, as recorded in the border defense files. During Zhao Erfeng's entry into Tibet, our tribe provided food and supplies, transporting approximately 5 million taels of silver before and after, and carrying weapons and arrows to guide the way, which has been resented by the Tibetan bandits. Therefore, the defeat of the border army affected our tribe, causing us to lose our land and country and causing tens of thousands of households and hundreds of thousands of people in our tribe to be occupied and slaughtered by Tibetan bandits to this day. Moreover, our tribe is closely connected to Tibet, guarding Xining and bordering Xikang. In the future, the China-Tibet Railway will be located in a vital area. For the sake of border defense, it is essential to make plans without delay. If the government is to rectify the border defenses and plan the administration, then our tribesmen, as border residents living in the border areas, should establish an office in Beijing to facilitate consultations and provide advice. There seems to be no reason to reject this request. Moreover, our tribe has defended the border for China, causing us to be resented by the Tibetan bandits, losing our land and homes, and suffering under the enemy for more than ten years. The representative has risked his life to travel thousands of miles and has endured all kinds of hardships. If there is ultimately no solution, the representative alone is insignificant, but what about the hundreds of thousands of elders and children of our tribe who are suffering day and night, hoping for the government's rescue? Xikang is listed as an inland area and is allowed to have representatives. Why should our tribe, with its vast territory, admiration for righteousness, and sincere contributions, be placed outside the scope of consideration? Since arriving in Beijing, the representative has been anxiously thinking day and night about the creation of a border region, the reform of the innovative region, the management, the repelling of enemies, the pacification of bandits, and so on. The only way to start is for the government to pay attention to border defense and approve the establishment of an office before there is room for progress. Furthermore, the representative is very unfamiliar with the Chinese language and writing, so there are many errors in the previous submission. This statement is hereby combined and respectfully submitted for approval and compliance. Respectfully submitted by Peng Chu, representative of the people of the thirty-nine tribes in the northwest border of Kham and Tibet."

Mantetsu

The First Sound of the New Economic Policy 70

The All-Manchuria Japanese Timber Merchants Hold a Joint Meeting

A dispatch from Andong states that the counties of Tonghua, Kuandian, Huanren, Linjiang, Changbai, etc., in the upper reaches of the Yalu River, have deep mountains and dense forests and have long been areas that produce timber. No less than 100,000 people rely on this to make a living. Moreover, the timber produced in the Yalu and Hun River basins is of excellent quality and beauty, and it is supplied not only to major cities and ports in the country, but also to Japan and Korea. According to statistics, there are more than 20 Japanese and Chinese merchants in this port who operate in the timber business (commonly known as "liaozhan"), with Japanese merchants accounting for approximately half of the total. Although the amount of timber produced in the upper reaches of the river has decreased sharply since 1923, timber merchants can still make a profit. However, after the opening of the Jihai and Shenhai Railways in the past two years, the implementation of joint transportation has absorbed the transportation rights of northeastern South Manchuria. The timber produced in the Hun River basin is not transported through the Yalu River, but directly to the interior by the Jihai and Shenhai Railways. In addition, the rising gold prices have caused the South Manchuria Railway's freight rates to increase invisibly by more than two times. All Manchurian Japanese timber merchants have been the first to bear the brunt of the impact, and their businesses have declined sharply. Recently, in order to reverse the decline of the timber industry, the Japanese Timber Merchants Association in the Andong Concession has initiated the All-Manchuria Timber Merchants Association. All timber merchants have unanimously agreed, and it was decided to hold the meeting from the 7th to the 9th of August at the Gongban Tong Gonghuitang in the Andong Concession. At that time, more than 30 timber merchant representatives from 16 places, including Fengcheng, Qiaotou, Benxi, Shenyang, Fushun, Tieling, Sipingjie, Changchun, Liaoyang, Yingkou, Xiong'yue, Wafangdian, Huashu, Jinzhou, Dalian, and Lushun, attended the meeting. The following five proposals were passed: (1) Abolish the Korean bonded factory. (2) Reduce the Mantetsu freight rates to counter the Jihai and Shenhai Railways. (3) Restore the Mantetsu construction petition that was terminated. (4) Mantetsu and other affiliated companies should use timber from the upper reaches of the river. (5) Korean railway freight rates should be reduced across the board.

It is reported that the main reason for the All-Manchuria Timber Merchants' meeting in Andong was that the newly appointed President of Mantetsu, Uchida, urgently wanted to implement a new economic policy to save Mantetsu's decline. Because the timber merchants' relationship with the economy is very large, he first gathered all the Manchurian timber merchants in Andong to organize a joint meeting. Andong is a suitable location because of its convenient transportation, and officials and businessmen from all walks of life in Korea can also participate conveniently. It is also heard that President Uchida specified that the proposals passed at this meeting should not conflict with the new economic policy. It is also heard that there were many attendees from all parties at this meeting. Guests included Andong Consul Mizusawa, Kwantung Government Official Muraki, Mantetsu Director Kato, Andong Police Chief Takayama, Lumber Company Director Yagi, Lumber Company Chief of General Affairs Hashimoto, Day Company's Yoshida and Iino Sales Section Chiefs, Chamber of Commerce President Arakawa, Local Committee Chairman Otsu, Andong Shinpo President Kawagoe, Kokkyo Mainichi Shimbun President Yoshinaga, Andong Station Freight Section Chief Nonaka, and Shoko Club's Asakura and Andong Station Chief Chiba. It can be seen that the Japanese attach great importance to this meeting. After the representatives of all parties closed the meeting on the 19th, they left An on the evening train. (10th)

The Jiangsu Provincial Representative Assembly Adjourned Yesterday 71

The Preliminary Meeting will Continue This Morning, and the First General Assembly will be Held This Afternoon

The Second Jiangsu Provincial Kuomintang Provincial Representative Assembly held its opening ceremony on the morning of the 15th and a preparatory meeting in the afternoon. The preparatory meeting was originally scheduled to produce all special committee members, but because of an error in the vote count for the presidium of the general assembly, it was delayed until approximately 5:00 PM before it was determined that Ge Jianshi, Zhang Renjie, and Zhang Minquan had been elected. By that time, it was time to adjourn the meeting, so an adjournment was announced.

The 16th was a Sunday, and the assembly announced a one-day recess. On the morning of the 17th, the second preparatory meeting will continue, scheduled to (1) elect the members of the General Assembly Proposal Review Committee, (2) elect the members of the General Assembly Declaration Drafting Committee, and (3) elect the members of the General Assembly Resolution Organizing Committee. The first general assembly will be held in the afternoon.

Local Correspondences

Fengxian 72

Lu Yaosheng, a Major Bandit in Jiangsu, Captured. Lu Yaosheng, a notorious bandit chief who roamed Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces (i.e., Taibao Ashu's Deputy General), fled to the coastal areas of Fengxian, Songjiang, and Nanhui counties with his followers after his accomplices Zhu Luo and Taibao Ashu were successively executed, creating disturbances. Although the Songjiang-Jinshan-Jiading-Pinghu Bandit Suppression Command offered a reward of 800 yuan for his capture, the bandit frequently sailed the seas, making it difficult to apprehend him. Now, County Police Chief Ding Zhiyan learned of the bandit's whereabouts through reconnaissance and led the Browning pistol team leader Zhu Wenyu, along with police officers, in a surprise attack last night (the 14th). He was captured at the home of salt farmer Chen Shuiqing at the foot of the Qin Gong Seawall outside the Taoist temple. He confessed to the crimes of robbing officials and looting, burning, and plundering in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces for the past three years. At the same time, the team also rescued Yang Meimei, a male hostage, from the empty house behind Chen's house. According to his confession, he was 20 years old, from Yaozhuang Bridge, Jiashan, Zhejiang, and was kidnapped by the bandit for ransom. This morning, Captain Ding prepared the documents and escorted him to the county government for interrogation and handling.

Wheat and Grain Association Allocates Funds to Purchase Grain: The County Wheat and Grain Association is now preparing to purchase grain for storage as the new grain is about to be harvested. Therefore, the association submitted a request to the county government to allocate all of the accumulated grain mu tax from the 19th year of the Republic for this purpose. In addition to the 6,640 yuan already received from the grain counters, there is still 2,216 yuan outstanding. A letter was sent to the Finance Bureau today requesting that it find a way to raise funds to meet the needs.

Kunshan 73

Provincial Security Team Captures Bandit in Kunshan: The Baoshan County Provincial Security Office captured a bandit named Fang Zhengshan a few days ago. He confessed that he was a scout in the bandit gang and claimed that the main bandit ship was currently anchored near Zhengyi. Upon receiving this information, the office dispatched the sixth company of the second battalion, led by company commander Chen Jiayi, along with Fang Zhengshan and more than 30 armed plainclothes soldiers, to Zhengyi by car on the morning of the 15th. They then boarded a boat and headed towards this county, arriving at Xiaoximen outside the city at 4:00 PM. Fang pointed out a boat ahead as a bandit ship. The soldiers ordered the boat to stop and searched it thoroughly. Finding no contraband, they detained the boat and captured Bao Jinzhang, his son, and his wife and daughter, totaling five people. They were then escorted to the county government. After interrogation by Examiner Chen, Bao Jinzhang and his son claimed that they made a living buying and selling lilies in Wuxi, Suzhou, and this county, and denied being bandits. Fang Zhengshan claimed that he made a living begging and was later captured by bandits and used as a scout. He also accused Bao of being Chen Dehai, who had robbed Baoshan, Jiading, Qingpu, and other places, but he himself had never participated in any robberies. The testimonies given before and after were quite inconsistent and incoherent. After the interrogation, an order was issued to Chen's company to escort Bao Jinzhang and his family back to Baoshan by night train at 7:00 PM for further investigation.

Qingpu 74

Captured Kidnapper Escapes: The kidnapper Zhu, also known as Ah Si, lived near Nijiabang in Beixiacun. The Water Police Division learned of his return and ordered the first detachment of the second district, stationed in Zhujiajiao, to arrest him. Yesterday, Ah Si was captured while drinking tea at the Ruiyuelou by the detachment, and he was detained on a patrol boat next to the detachment headquarters. It was planned to escort him to the county government for legal action in the afternoon. However, the suspect took advantage of the police officers' inattention and swam away. By the time it was discovered, he had disappeared without a trace.

A Soil Trafficker Escapes in the Middle of the Night: Gu Yinglian, a patrol officer from the Huangdu Public Security Sub-Bureau in the 10th district of this county, received a report that soil traffickers Tian and Hu were transporting a large amount of opium to Huangdu. After receiving the report, Officer Gu personally led police officers to the pier to investigate. They found two men with suspicious behavior carrying a package. After questioning by Officer Gu, the package was opened and found to contain more than ten jin of opium. One person took the opportunity to escape, and only one soil trafficker was captured. He confessed that he was a retired police officer. Both the soil trafficker and the opium were detained overnight, and it was planned to transfer them to the county government for legal action the next day. However, the suspect had disappeared, and the police officers on duty were also missing.

Nanhui 75

A Wife's Licentiousness Leads to a Husband's Prank: The wife, Qiu, of Mei Kuishu, the owner of the Yongyuanxiang shoe store in the North Gate of the city, was middle-aged but still licentious. Kuishu had repeatedly warned her to no avail and was quite angry. Last night, while his wife was sound asleep, he suddenly used an iron bar used for making shoes to violently insert into his wife's private parts. Blood immediately flowed all over the bed, and she lost consciousness. Neighbors and shopkeepers learned of this incident and immediately reported it to the Public Security Bureau, who detained Mei for questioning. Qiu was taken to the First Public Hospital for treatment. It is said that her injuries are very serious and her life is in danger.

Wuxi 76

Major Fire Outside the West Gate: Dozens of Jiangbei shacks behind Xinxinyuan on Huang Lane outside the West Gate of this county suddenly caught fire due to carelessness in a certain shack yesterday morning (the 16th) at 1:00 AM, causing a conflagration. Thick smoke filled the air, and the flames burst through the roofs. Upon hearing the alarm, nearby fire brigades rushed to the scene and tried their best to extinguish the fire. It took more than an hour to put out the fire, but dozens of thatched shacks had been completely destroyed. At the time of the fire, laborers cried out and wailed, and their situation was very tragic.

Bandits Kidnap Child, Neighbors Rescue Him: Xia Hezheng's home in Xialianqiao, Xialian Township, 11th district (South Yanshi) was robbed by bandits in February of this year. Xia Hezheng's younger brother was also seriously injured by the bandits. A message was received that six or seven bandits, dressed in short clothes and armed with iron rulers and flashlights, broke open the gate and rushed into the house again yesterday. They kidnapped Xia Hezheng's son, Weisheng (12 years old). Xia Hezheng's wife saw that her beloved son was kidnapped and immediately chased him out of the door, grabbing hold of the bandits and refusing to let go, resulting in her being beaten and injured by the bandits. Neighbors learned of this and came to the rescue, successfully rescuing Weisheng. It was fortunate indeed.

Demanding Debt Unsuccessfully Leads to Death: Wu Anan, a resident of Xuelianqiao Town West Street, located at the junction of Wuxi and Changzhou, is inherently fierce. He is currently running a small shop in the town. Recently, Gong Genquan, a villager from Jixiang Township, borrowed two yuan and eight jiao from Anan. A few days ago, Anan demanded the debt from Genquan but was unsuccessful. He then summoned several locals to Gong's house to demand the debt. Genquan, unable to bear the pressure, was overcome with despair and jumped into the nearby river. No one rescued him, resulting in his drowning. The deceased's father, Songquan, learned of the news and negotiated with Anan, eventually settling the matter for fifty yuan. Poor Gong Genquan is now lying underground in his coffin.

Rape of Daughter Case Heard Again: Ah Xi, the 16-year-old daughter of Xie Daishi, a resident of the Taifu silk factory workshop on Tatangxia outside the South Gate of this county, was raped in the spring of this year by Xie Daishi's lover, Ye Ziping (61 years old), who broke into her room. Ashamed and indignant, Ah Xi threw herself into the river, but fortunately, she was rescued before drowning. The police officers from the Third Branch detained Ye Ziping and escorted him to the county court for questioning and detention. It is now known that the case was scheduled for a hearing again yesterday. The plaintiff Xie Daishi, Xie Axi, and witness Yang Naidong were present. At 10:00 AM, Judge Liang ascended the third criminal court and brought in Ye Ziping, who was in custody. During the hearing, Xie and her daughter firmly stated that Ye Ziping came to rape Ah Xi, and Ah Xi firmly refused. Xu Jinxiu and Zhang Aqiao, who were sleeping with Ah Xi at the time, saw this behavior and reprimanded him. Ah Xi then jumped into the river out of anger, and so on. When questioned, Ye Ziping did not admit to the rape. Next, witness Yang Naidong made a statement. The defendant's appointed lawyer, Sun Zuhong, stood up and stated his defense intentions, requesting that Xie Axi be sent to the hospital for an examination to determine if she was a virgin before further investigation was conducted. Judge Liang approved the request and ordered that Xie Axi be sent to Tongren Hospital for examination. Xie Daishi and Yang Naidong were dismissed, and Ye Ziping was returned to custody to await a further hearing.

Zhenjiang 77

Unscrupulous Merchants Hoarding Rice: The First District Office of Zhenjiang County reported to the Township Offices in the Southeast Gate area that it had recently discovered that rice merchants outside the South Gate were privately hoarding rice transported from the countryside by villagers and reselling it to rice merchants outside the West Gate for transportation out of the county, causing rice prices to skyrocket. The most bizarre thing is that poor people in the southeast are being refused when they go to buy even a small amount of rice. The Third Sub-Association of the Autonomy Research Association has sent letters to the First and Third Public Security Branches, ordering them to send police officers to notify the rice merchants in the South Gate that they must not refuse retail sales. The First District Office has reported the situation to the county government and requested that it issue a notice prohibiting hoarding and prohibiting transportation out of the county. A letter has also been sent to the Rice Industry Association to inform the rice merchants to comply in order to avoid causing a rice shortage.

Captured Soldiers Escorted to Zhenjiang: Ouyang Zhen, the commander of the Special Service Regiment of the Guard Army, escorted more than 1,500 captured soldiers from the front line yesterday by train from Nanjing to Zhenjiang and sent them to the 35th Battalion outside the South Gate for resettlement.

Jiangyin 78

A wife has an affair, and a child is murdered. Qin Xiangbao's wife, of San Guan Township, Xin Jing Bridge, was having an affair with her clan uncle, A Lin. The husband negotiated with the adulterer three times at the San Guan Temple, settling the matter for eighty silver dollars. Later, A Lin regretted it. On the fourteenth night, Xiangbao returned home and argued with his wife, then used a kitchen knife to chop his three-year-old son to death. His wife then reported the crime to the Second Sub-Bureau of Public Security, and A Lin was arrested and sent to the county for legal proceedings.

Bandits sought money in the town and requested that they be brought in. Gu Gengquan's grandson, of Gu Shunfeng Lumber Mill in Qin Nan Shuang Jing Gate, was kidnapped on the night of June 25th. A ransom of seven thousand silver dollars was demanded. After the district's first A-level regiment was notified, several people, including Wang Laoer, were apprehended and detained. Later, an informant in Dan Yang Ling Kou identified Dai Yinshi. It was learned that the bandits were hiding in the Xin Feng area. Subsequently, the local militia apprehended five members of the Xing Hui Xiang Xing Da Hui family: Sun Da Ji, Lao Da, Liu Da Sheng and his son. They were sent to the Zhenjiang Security Office, where the military court interrogated them and confronted them with the informant before detaining them. On the 15th, the district regiment submitted a request to the county government to prepare a document to Zhenjiang to bring them in.

Danyang 79

Robbery and assault by bandits in Wulonggang. On the night before last, at 9 p.m., the home of farmer Fu Shuangjing in Wulonggang, western township, was suddenly entered by a group of bandits who dug a hole in the back door. The bandits ransacked the house and abducted Fu's four-year-old child, fleeing towards the southeast. Upon hearing the alarm, the First Police Squad of the garrison in Fengluo Village rushed to the scene, but the bandits had already fled. Only one suspect, Li Yushan, was apprehended in a melon field and has been sent to the county for interrogation.

The Provincial Committee came to Danyang to investigate a case. Previously, in the twelfth district of this county, the excavation of the Jiuqu River during the spring floods caused the flooding of farmland, inciting farmers to gather and destroy the houses of various section chiefs. Subsequently, the victims filed a petition with the provincial and county governments requesting compensation and punishment. The county government, upon receiving the petition, arrested Yao Jian and others and detained them for investigation. Now, the provincial government has specially dispatched Commissioner Wang Jigang to Danyang today to investigate the case in detail and handle it.

Nantong 80

Bandits are harassing the eastern townships. Recently, large groups of bandits have infiltrated the Xinhe Town area of the Si Jia Ba in the eastern townships of Nantong, setting fires, looting, and kidnapping people. The police and militia joined forces to suppress them, but the bandits relied on the tall green crops for cover and resisted the police and militia until dawn before retreating. Many anti-government leaflets were found in the town, and a temporary curfew was declared in all districts.

Resignation of the County Court President. Jian Jiong, the president of the Nantong County Court, has resigned to the Ministry of Judicial Administration because the court's funds are exhausted, the detention center is facing a food shortage, and he is unable to maintain it. He has been transferred to the Second Civil Court of the Shanghai District Court. Jian returned to Nantong on the 15th to handle the handover. His successor has not yet been appointed.

Yan Zheming's coffin will be exhumed for examination. The Provincial Public Security Water Police Team stationed in Tong arbitrarily shot and killed Yan Zheming in front of the court. The Prosecutor's Office is investigating the case in accordance with the law and has sent a letter to the Water Police Team headquarters, pointing out that Yan Zheming's coffin is buried so that it can be exhumed for examination.

Surplus police officers sent back to their hometowns. The Nantong County Police Force has reduced its annual budget by 14,000 yuan and laid off more than 100 surplus police officers, sending them back to their hometowns.

Yangzhou 81

A record of visiting the canal flood. The canal water level is spreading, and the Zhaoguan Dam is in imminent danger. This is an unprecedented sight since the collapse of the Gaoyan Dam during the Xianfeng era of the Qing Dynasty, more than 80 years ago. The reporter, recognizing the severity of the disaster, attached a special transport vessel from the Construction Bureau and traveled north to observe the situation. The riverfront houses on both sides were deeply submerged in water, reaching the bay head. The water to the north was even more turbulent. The turbulent currents beneath the Bihu Bridge were deep and forceful, eroding the banks with waves reaching six feet high. All the ships traveling to and fro hugged the west bank, and rowing upstream required thirty to forty people to pull the tow ropes. The high mound on the west bank of the Wayaopu had become a level embankment. Further north, the lakes and waters on both sides were boundless, with only the rooftops of houses floating on the water. The water at the Yidu pier in the Chenjia Gou of the Liuzha Gate was level with the plaque of each memorial archway. Only the top of the Liuzha Jiaoguan Pavilion was visible. The dike willows and the Zhong Da Wang Temple on the west bank were all submerged in the Dragon Palace. Only strands of willow branches swayed in the waves. Along the eastern embankment, for seven or eight li, thousands of people gathered, carrying baskets and soil, frantically running about. The old embankment was submerged, and the new revetment only protruded five inches above the water. The sound of emergency repairs never ceased. The next morning, upon arriving at the Zhaoguan Dam, more than 2,000 people had gathered on the dam because they had heard rumors of the dam being opened. Therefore, in addition to the farmers from the nearby Xiaqiao Township, Zhenwu Temple, and Qiaoshu area, people from Taidong Xing and other counties also came, carrying farming tools and baskets of grain, sitting on mats and assisting in carrying soil to fill the dike. Representatives from the local county government also stationed themselves at the construction site to supervise the work. On the evening of the 12th, Li Mingyang, a member of the Provincial Committee, arrived at the dam with a company of guards and rested at the Sanyuan Temple. The crowd was greatly alarmed, mistaking it for the opening of the dam, and immediately beat gongs and gathered 5,000 people, vowing to protect it with their lives. After the district chief, Yang, declared the intention to protect the dike, the suspicion remained unresolved and did not dissipate overnight. When Li went to Shaoji to discuss raising funds to quickly build a new revetment and saw Li heading to the post office, the people's hearts were finally set at ease.

Gaoyou 82

The recent disaster situation in Gaoyou. Since the opening of the Guihai Three Dams, the loss of farmland in the lower reaches of this county has been extremely severe. Since the 8th of this month, a strong southeast wind has suddenly sprung up and has continued to this day. This wind is very favorable for the canal, so although there has been a source of water recently, there has been no major increase in the water level. However, the lower reaches have suffered greatly. Because the southeast wind blocked the dam water from flowing eastward smoothly, the fields and weirs near the city have been repeatedly endangered by the huge waves of the dam water in recent days. Last night (the 11th), the wind was particularly strong, and the Hengfeng, Langpi, Hexing, and Zhangshiliang weirs in the southern township were all breached by the huge waves, completely submerging the fields and crops. This morning, the Hucheng Weir Yangjia Bridge and Jujiada Bridge have been in danger more than ten times. At this moment, the Hucheng Weir is no longer in danger, but the Yangjia Bridge has collapsed for more than a zhang and cannot be repaired. The county government has transported thousands of sacks to the Jujiada Bridge and is still trying to repair it. Residents of this city, Zhao Wanru and Wang Yongwen, and others, because the victims of the various weirs have not eaten for several days, feel deeply saddened and specially solicited funds from various shops and residents to purchase several dan of dry food and went by boat to provide disaster relief yesterday afternoon. Unexpectedly, when the boat arrived at the Gaomiao Weir, the victims swarmed onto the boat before it could be distributed, snatching everything and knocking Zhao and others into the water. Fortunately, they were rescued and did not drown. The tragedy can be seen from this. The Red Cross Society of this city specially sent staff member Zhang Shihai to Lake West to rescue the victims. So far, a batch of 44 people has been transported to the Caishin Temple Lake West Refugee Camp in the city. The association has also sent people to the various weirs in the lower reaches to rescue the victims. However, because the houses of the victims have been submerged in water, but the rice, wheat, and other items in the houses have not been taken out, they are temporarily staying on the weir bank or under large trees to guard them and are unwilling to come to the city. The association has dispatched people to the lower reaches to salvage corpses because many people and animals have drowned.

Xuzhou 83

Newly appointed officials of the newly formed Sixth Division. Cheng Daizhou, the commander of the newly formed Sixth Division of the National Revolutionary Army, and Bai Lefu, the deputy commander, have been ordered to take office. They are actively preparing for internal organization. It is reported that yesterday, Zhou Liuwu was hired as a Major General Counselor of the Headquarters, Huang Tingyu was appointed as the Director of the Military Supply Department, Zheng Xitao as the Lieutenant Colonel Counselor, Zhang Chao as the Counselor, and Gao Gongxu, Gao Weixin, Yang Tinggui, Yan Chengquan and others as adjutants.

Hangzhou 84

Gambling case at the train station. The station master dismissed from his post. Li Bin, the stationmaster of Linping Station on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway, was arrested by the local Public Security Bureau last month for gambling under the platform with Lai Xilin, Chen Tonglin, and others, and was sent to the Hangzhou District Court for interrogation. After investigation by the Prosecutor's Office, it was confirmed that Lai Xilin and Chen Tonglin were guilty of gambling and were prosecuted. The Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway Administration also sent personnel to thoroughly investigate Li Bin. As a result, it was determined that the stationmaster had indeed violated the law and neglected his duties. Yesterday, an order was issued to dismiss Li from his post and deduct three months' salary as a warning.

The murderer appeals the verdict. Chu Xiaomao, a farmer from Xiaoshan, killed Tang Jinlin with a sharp weapon due to a gambling debt dispute. He was sentenced to twelve years of imprisonment by the county court. He appealed, and the High Court has now learned that the trial of the case resulted in the original sentence being too light and should be revoked and changed to thirteen years of imprisonment. He was ordered to be escorted back to the original county for execution yesterday.

Hangzhou tap water is officially supplied. After the full water test by the Hangzhou Tap Water Preparation Committee, the sludge in the water pipes has been repeatedly flushed clean in recent days. Yesterday, the official water supply has begun. Users who registered before the water supply and paid the deposit in accordance with the regulations will be exempt from water charges for one month. However, the eastern street area is still under construction because it is not a prosperous area.

Pinghu 85

Another robbery case near Xincang. Zhu Arong's family, located in the Li Jia Langxia of the Sanqing Port near Xincang in the eastern townships of Pinghu, was relatively well-off. On the night of the 12th, several robbers suddenly broke into Zhu's house and ransacked it at will. Zhu's daughter was scheduled to marry next month, and the dowry she had prepared was all robbed. The robbers stayed for three hours. However, Zhu's family had been robbed several times last year, and this loss was even greater than last year.

Police officers were suddenly arrested. Yesterday (the 15th), Zhang Afu, a police officer from the Xincang Public Security Sub-Bureau in Pinghu, whose family lived in the Luwan Temple in the eastern townships, was suddenly arrested by soldiers from the Jiangsu Provincial Security Team stationed in Qianjiawei Town, Jinshan. First, they guarded the Public Security Sub-Bureau, then entered and arrested Zhang Afu, and escorted him to Qianjiawei. It is said that the reason for the arrest was that he had colluded with bandits.

The Public Security Bureau Chief dismissed and investigated. Fang Menggeng, the Chief of the Pinghu Public Security Sub-Bureau, was previously the Chief of the Zhapu Sub-Bureau. A nameless floating corpse was found in the outer sea. It was said that it was carrying more than 1,300 yuan in cash. Fang did not report it to the county and buried it without permission. Later, County Chief Wu learned about it and sent someone to verify it. He then submitted it to the hall for review. It is now learned that the hall has ordered Fang to be investigated and that Zhang Huanwen, a staff member of the Qingxiang Bureau, has been appointed to fill the vacancy.

Shaoxing 86

Changes in the organization of tobacco and alcohol tax inspection. The Shaoxing Tobacco and Alcohol Bureau has been ordered to be renamed the Tax Inspection Branch Bureau, reducing the area of jurisdiction and dividing it for management. The inspection offices and inspection stations previously under its jurisdiction have also been changed and abolished. Inspection stations along the Yantang area, such as Xixing, have been abolished. An office will be established in Qianqing, a key export area of Shaoxing, to inspect goods shipped out. Inspection stations will still be established in Cao'e on the east and west routes of Shaoxing wine, and branch offices will be set up in other areas such as Wengang for patrol to prevent tax evasion.

The provincial government has approved the use of tin foil customs tax receipts to offset payments. Because tin foil from various Shaoxing foil shops must pass through customs and pay customs duties when shipped to other provinces, most of these taxes are required to offset the regular tax. Because the Jiangzhe foil special tax has been contracted by the foil merchants, there has been no solution to the customs tax issue, causing disputes from time to time. The Tax Contracting Association has submitted a petition to the Finance Office requesting assistance. It has now been ordered that customs duties collected by customs for foil that has been transported through customs after the special business tax has been paid be allowed to be submitted by the association for verification and deduction.

Anqing 87

Severely punish the derelict county magistrate. Wang Yunlong, the former county magistrate of Fuyang, has been removed from his post for dereliction of duty. The government has now handed him over to the court for investigation in accordance with the law. After Wang was removed from his post, he was handed over to Huaining County for custody and later released on bail. He has now been transferred to the court.

The Guangfeng Weir has collapsed again. The Qingfeng Weir in Duhu, on the north bank of the Yangtze River opposite Anqing, collapsed at 5 p.m. on the 10th due to excessive wind and waves. The Hucheng Weir in Anqing is also in constant danger. If the Hucheng Weir is not protected, boats could travel on land within the city of Anqing.

Bengbu 88

The weather is clear, and the water level is gradually receding. Previously, Bengbu had continuous heavy rain and a flood that turned the surrounding area into a vast expanse of water, almost a swamp. The water depth in the East and West Amusement Parks, as well as Guozhi Street, Huachang Street, Taiping Street, and Xin Da Ma Road, ranged from two to three feet to four to five feet. In the past few days, the weather has been clear and hot, and the water level has receded. Dry land has appeared in Huachang Street, Lao Da Jie, and other areas. The water in the East and West Amusement Parks has receded by two to three feet. Many of those who had taken refuge from the water have returned home to repair their houses. However, the crops in the four rural areas have all been flooded and killed, making it difficult to harvest anything in the autumn. The disaster victims are now clamoring for relief.

Bandits in Fengtai. Large groups of bandits, including communists, have been found in the Tianjiaji area of Fengtai County, northern Anhui Province. They are manipulating and commanding, committing arson, murder, robbery, and all sorts of evil deeds. At the beginning of the month, the Changhuai Water Public Security Bureau's water patrol team, the Huaiyuan Security Regiment, the Shouxian Provisional Second Brigade, and the Independent Battalion joined forces to suppress them. Although the bandits suffered setbacks, they have not been completely eliminated. Recently, they have mixed with nearby water bandits and are accustomed to intercepting merchant ships on the water, making them very rampant. Xia Futang, the county magistrate of Fengtai, is preparing to lead the police to suppress them and has specially sent a letter to the Bengbu Public Security Bureau requesting that they seal two small steamships to be used in order to advance by land and water and eliminate them in one fell swoop.

Letter

Letter from Zhang Wenyao, Head of the Third District of Songjiang County 89

I recently praised your newspaper's Songjiang communication column for publishing an article entitled "Dismantling Aircraft Creates Complications," which is completely inconsistent with the facts. On the morning of August 12th, after 8 a.m., a Jiangpeng aircraft landed in the Hebang Township area, damaging more than one mu of autumn rice in the field of villager Zhang Xuanchun. Mr. Zhang claimed compensation for the loss. Subsequently, He Jian, the aircraft instructor, asked the district office to mediate and ordered the police to protect the aircraft to avoid further losses. The district chief and Assistant Han cordially entertained him and urged Officer Xu to send police to protect the aircraft. They also persuaded Mr. Zhang to accept 20 yuan in compensation to resolve the matter peacefully. On the evening of the 13th, the aircraft was dismantled and transported to the Xinqiao Station for shipment to the Hongqiao Airport for repair. There was no fact that Assistant Han demanded 200 yuan in compensation. On the morning of the 14th, at 9 a.m., Officer Xu Guodong of the Tenth Sub-Bureau, due to illiteracy and improper handling, was criticized by Assistant Han. Holding a grudge, he fabricated facts and reported to his superior, leading a group of armed police to illegally coerce and attempt to arrest Assistant Han, interfering with his freedom. At that time, half of the district was agitated. When the district chief heard the news, he rushed to the scene and argued reasonably. As a result, he and Assistant Han each appealed to the higher authorities. Xu's transfer and Han's fake resignation have already aroused public outrage in the entire district, and they have sent telegrams to the Ministry of Interior and the Department of Civil Affairs requesting a thorough investigation. I am writing this special letter to request that you investigate and correct the facts to reveal the truth. With great respect, Zhang Wenyao, Head of the Third District of Songjiang County, August 15th.

Central Educational and Cultural Expenses for the 19th Year 91

Recurrent expenses: 14,422,475 yuan

Temporary expenses: 299,400 yuan

The central educational and cultural expenses are subject to review and compilation by the Ministry of Education, and include all expenses related to the Ministry of Education, the Academia Sinica, national schools, libraries, museums, and other central cultural institutions and cultural facilities. The budget estimate for the 20th year was reviewed and compiled in May and sent to the Directorate-General of Budget, Accounting and Statistics. However, the annual budget is usually approved and promulgated before the start of the year. The central education budget for the 20th year has not yet been announced, and the central government has issued a temporary remedy to be used as a temporary measure. The Ministry of Education has been ordered to instruct all subordinate agencies to comply with this. The approved amounts for the 19th year are classified and explained as follows:

(1) School Operating Expenses 92

The recurrent expenses for Central University are 1,956,000 yuan; for Jinan University, 630,664 yuan; for Labor University, 645,268 yuan, with temporary expenses of 40,000 yuan; for Tongji University, 445,900 yuan, with temporary expenses of 91,400 yuan; for Zhejiang University, 769,095 yuan; for Wuhan University, 660,000 yuan; for Qingdao University, 420,000 yuan; for Sun Yat-sen University, 1,500,000 yuan; for the Art College, 100,800 yuan; for the Music College, 60,000 yuan; for the Beiping Mongolian-Tibetan School, 100,000 yuan, with temporary expenses of 18,000 yuan; for Beiping University, 1,885,704 yuan; for Peking University, 1,020,000 yuan; for Beiping Normal University, 598,296 yuan; for Beiyang Institute of Technology, 276,000 yuan; for the Supplementary School attached to the Panchen Lama's Office in Beijing, 17,808 yuan. In addition, the recurrent expenses for the Sino-French National Institute of Technology, which are shared equally by China and France, are 85,000 yuan. The total approved recurrent expenses are 11,177,735 yuan, and the temporary expenses are 149,400 yuan.

(2) Central Education Subsidies 93

The maintenance fee for cultural institutions is 60,000 yuan; for the Central Guoshu Institute, 60,000 yuan; and subsidies for other universities and colleges, 360,000 yuan. The total approved amount is 480,000 yuan.

(3) Various Expenses for Central Educational and Cultural Institutions and Cultural Facilities 94

The recurrent expenses for the Academia Sinica are 1,320,000 yuan; for the Beiping Research Institute, 360,000 yuan; for the Nanjing Ancient Artifact Preservation Institute, 2,400 yuan; for the Chinese Dictionary Compilation Office attached to the National Language Unification Preparatory Committee, 20,000 yuan; for the Ancient Artifact Preservation Committee, 12,000 yuan; for the Central Education Hall, 50,000 yuan, with temporary expenses of 70,000 yuan; for the Guangdong-Guangxi Geological Survey Institute, 48,000 yuan; for study abroad expenses, 33,996 yuan; and the central education reserve fund is 360,000 yuan. The total approved recurrent expenses are 2,206,396 yuan, and the temporary expenses are 70,000 yuan.

(4) Expenses for the Ministry of Education, the Beiping Archives Preservation Office, and the Overseas Student Supervision Office 95

The recurrent expenses for the Ministry of Education are 504,000 yuan, with temporary expenses of 80,000 yuan; for the Beiping Archives Preservation Office, 6,744 yuan; and for the Overseas Student Supervision Office, 47,600 yuan. The total approved recurrent expenses are 558,344 yuan, and the temporary expenses are 80,000 yuan.

In summary, the total approved education and culture expenses for the 19th year are 14,422,475 yuan for recurrent expenses and 299,400 yuan for temporary expenses.

Efforts to Rescue Jiangsu Education Funds 96

Sharp Reduction in Land Tax - Meeting to Discuss

Zhenjiang, 16th: The Jiangsu Province's education budget for the 20th year has already been resolved by the Funding Committee. Recently, due to the province's unusually severe floods, the sharp reduction in land tax has affected the source of education funds. The Jiangsu Education Department, for the sake of prudence, specially sent a letter yesterday requesting the Education Funding Committee to convene another meeting to discuss rapid relief measures.

Good News for Weihai Students 97

Re-election by the Commissioner's Office to Send Outstanding Students to Higher Education

Xu Yanmou, the Special Commissioner of Weihai, has spared no effort in improving local education in his daily work. In less than a year, he has been able to transform it. For 32 years under British rule, a policy of keeping the people ignorant was maintained. All schools were either private schools of the absolutely laissez-faire type or missionary schools of cultural aggression. As a result, the atmosphere was closed, almost like being outside the pale of civilization. Only after the recovery was it possible to make major reforms, such as banning private schools, screening private school teachers, delineating school districts, opening schools in various villages, testing primary school teachers, recruiting educational talent, establishing the First Middle School, and implementing Party-oriented education. The educational circle in Weihai has undergone fundamental transformation through this vigorous and earnest implementation, and a vibrant atmosphere has gradually taken shape. Recently, in order to support talent, Special Commissioner Xu has raised funds and stipulated measures to send Weihai students to higher education. A total of 20 places have been allocated for middle schools, universities, and vocational schools. Examinations were held twice in late July to select outstanding students to send to higher education.

Xu Peihuang and Others Give Speeches

Yesterday afternoon at 4:30 p.m., the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau, the Universal Chinese Student Association, Jiaotong University, the Business School of Central University, Jinan University, Labor University, Guanghua University, the Law School of Soochow University, Qixiu Girls' School, and the Middle

Seventeen organizations, including the National Science Society, Tsinghua Alumni Association, China Vocational Education Society, China Institute in America, The Republican Daily News, The China Critic Weekly, The Commercial Press, and China Bookstore, held a farewell party at the Chen Family Garden at No. 6 Seymour Road for students going abroad. The United States in Irreversible Decline 112

Singles Losses Lead to Total Elimination

Canada's Devaux Completes Great Feat 113

(7-5)

Devaux (Canada) (6-2) Squiers (USA)

(6-0)

Canada's victory over the United States was expected. The United States' defeat in all three groups over two days led to their total elimination, a disappointing irreversible decline. Yesterday's singles match between Canada and the United States initially saw some struggle, but it gradually became unsustainable, ultimately leading to a complete collapse. Devaux's skill was indeed superior to Squiers. At the beginning of the first set, Squiers was agile and dynamic, like a dragon gaining power and eclipsing the world. However, he became careless when leading 5-4, and missed a good opportunity. His 5-7 loss was regretted by the entire audience. In the second set, Squiers performed worse than before, managing only to defend without making any progress. In the third set, Devaux became stronger, and Squiers' technique became more chaotic, ultimately leading to a "bagel" set loss. Canada's Devaux completed a great feat in the opening round and will soon compete with China. Because the outcome has been decided, the remaining doubles and singles groups between Canada and the United States will not be held.

Intense Battle Still to Come Between England and Japan 114

Japan Leads, England Determined to Fight Back

Japan's Strong Doubles Team Defeats England 115

Hyotare Kumagai (6-2) Tuckey

(Japan) (6-3) (England)

Machida (6-1) Masters

The Japanese doubles team of Hyotare Kumagai and Machida is well-known for its strength. Kumagai's comprehensive coverage can compensate for Machida's shortcomings. The English doubles team of Masters is not famous in history, but his consistent performance is remarkable. After intense battles, the veteran Tuckey was lacking in stamina. At the beginning of the match, the English doubles team repeatedly approached the net to attack, but the Japanese were cunning and broke through with a high lob. Unable to succeed, England lost four games in a row. Masters' cannonball serves won back a game. After winning another game, they lost two more in a row, suffering a 2-6 defeat. From the second set onwards, the Japanese continued to control the field, and the English had no way to fight back. They quickly completed the set with six consecutive games. The power of the Japanese was evident. In the sixth game, Kumagai launched a fierce attack, but he was too hasty, and the ball went out of bounds, giving England a game. England's momentum gradually increased, and they seized the opportunity to counterattack. The two players defended closely at the net, attacking left and right to their heart's content, winning three games. Masters' serves continued to be powerful, and Kumagai turned the situation around, securing the victory with a score of 6-3. In the third set, the Japanese were unstoppable and invincible. Soon, they succeeded with a score of 6-1. Tomorrow, England and Japan still have two singles groups to play: England's Wheatley against Japan's Kumagai, and Japan's Machida against England's Tuckey. Judging by the overall situation, Japan is likely to win, but the English are determined to put up a strong fight in the hope of a miracle.

Commercial News

Gold Prices Continued to Rise Last Week 116

A Strong Upward Trend. Last week, the trend of gold prices became even stronger, reaching 780 taels at one point. Following a gradual path, it almost had a strong upward trend. It began to rise sharply at the beginning of the week, and then fluctuated constantly, creating a revolving situation, hovering above 70 taels. During the week, there was a review of 30 taels, and a total increase of 24 taels was calculated. This was because the US government released the US cotton estimate, and although prices had fallen, there was still concern that it would affect the silver market. In addition, due to the mixed international news, people were restless. The prices of silver in England, the United States, India, and Shanghai exchange were all firming up, and the exchange rates of English in the internal market were high for those who shorted silver. Therefore, the market price became increasingly tight, and even broke through one shilling and three pence. At the end of the week, the rollover for October arrived. The shorts still paid a premium of 3 taels and 2 or 3 mace to 3 taels, but the shorts had plenty of spot goods, so the rollover was raised. The transaction volume of the exchange was only about 30,000, and the opening price for October was 776 taels, which once reached 80 taels and 0.08 qian, and closed at 78 taels and a half. As for the closing price, calculated according to the daily exchange rate, the road for the day seemed to become more active and the price increased by about 10 taels. However, there was no significant outflow of large silver, and there was no increase or decrease in yesterday's (16th) telegram. The future of gold prices may still fluctuate. The details of the week's developments are summarized below.

A glimpse of the forward process. Since Monday (August 10), large silver has shrunk by 125, and the silver price has shrunk by 25. The shilling exchange rate has not changed at first, but has been changed three times, a total of one and a half gears (375). As the internal market became increasingly tight, the shorts were eager to cover. The opening price of gold for September was 56 taels and a half, an initial increase of 4 taels and 7 qian. US cotton suffered a severe drop, but due to the excitement of buyers, the price suddenly rose. In the afternoon, it peaked at 80 taels and closed at 77 taels and 6 qian, a sharp increase of 25 taels and 8 qian compared to last Saturday. Throughout the day, there was a total of 24 taels of difference. Speculator Mr. Wu came and went again, while Mr. Lu bought in general. The shorts rushed to cover. Yarn Prices Plunge by Four to Five Taels Last Week 120

Yarn prices plummeted last week due to the larger than expected bumper crop of US cotton, throwing the world cotton market into disarray. The local market became increasingly apprehensive, and the sharp decline in prices created a sense of freefall. Actual demand was increasingly weak, and even though the kebang [native place guilds] attempted to buy, they held back due to the unfavorable situation. As a result, trading was also shut down. On Monday, yarn prices dropped by five to six taels, triggering profit-taking and bargain hunting, which stabilized the situation somewhat. However, a certain major merchant's sentiment remained depressed, and he was willing to sell at 145 taels. When prices rose, he still shorted. At the weekend, there was some trading in coarse yarn by the Yunnan and Guangdong kebang, and the Sichuan kebang also saw some activity, tightening the market slightly. Yarn prices rebounded by two to three taels. As a result, prices for all months fell by four to five taels compared to the previous week. Cotton Market Plunges Sharply Last Week 121

US Cotton Delivers a Major Blow

The cotton market experienced a sharp decline last week as the US government's cotton production estimate exceeded expectations, causing panic among cotton merchants worldwide. At a time when consumption in various countries is weak, the bumper crop will be unmanageable in the future. As a result, Japanese merchants such as Dongmian liquidated their long positions one after another, and retail investors panicked, causing the market to plummet. On Thursday, news came that the US Agricultural Adjustment Administration had proposed destroying one-third of the new cotton, which slightly stirred the market and led to a rebound of 5 qian. However, major traders took advantage of the rise to sell in large quantities, and most manufacturers bought cheap US cotton to hedge against standard cotton, as local cotton was several taels higher than US cotton. Some believed that after the sharp fall in US cotton, there would be a period of consolidation. The severe floods in various regions would affect the new cotton, tightening the long positions and unwilling to let go. However, the overall situation of the world cotton industry is pessimistic, and the surplus abroad is disheartening. The outlook is mostly bearish. The price of standard cotton fell by 1 tael and 8.9 qian compared to the previous week. The total transaction volume was 1,000,034. However, the active trading volume set a new record. Factories bought 20,000 to 30,000 cheap US cotton, with 1,300 bales from Yao cotton. US cotton fell by more than 100 pounds compared to last week. Flood Relief Committee Organized and Established Yesterday 135

Presumed Heads of Each Group Discussed Bylaws and Important Cases

The National Government Flood Relief Committee, which was officially announced by the National Government on the 14th of this month, was convened by Chairman Song Ziwen in Shanghai at 9:00 a.m. yesterday (the 16th). Attendees included Xu Shiying, Kong Xiangxi, Wang Boqun, Zhang Gongquan, Liu Ruiheng, Niu Huisheng, as well as Treasury Department Advisor Younger, and Railway Ministry Advisor Baker. The committee's charter was first proposed for discussion and approval. The names of the heads of each group were also presumed as follows: Director of the Investigation Group and Secretary-General Zeng Rongpu; Director of the Finance Group Song Ziwen; Director of the Accounting Audit Group Zhang Gongquan; Director of the Health and Epidemic Prevention Group Liu Ruiheng; Director of the Transportation Group Yu Qiaqing; Director of the Liaison Group Kong Xiangxi; Director of the Disaster Area Work Zhu Qinglan. In addition, there were public discussions and resolutions on various cases listed on the left: (1) To hire famous figures from China and abroad as additional members of the committee. Once their consent is obtained, the list of names can be announced. (2) To establish a standing committee to handle all committee affairs, organized by five special government commissioners and a number of additional members. (3) To jointly conduct investigations with the Yangtze River Water Conservancy Commission, the Huai River Regulation Commission, the Dredging Bureau, various engineers, and surveying experts. Currently, the disaster situation in Hankou is the most severe. The committee has entrusted Liu Ruiheng, Baker, and Stottpe to fly to Hankou to coordinate with various parties to handle emergency relief and sanitation matters there, and to inspect the disaster situation near Hankou by flying over it and provide a factual report. (4) To invite various relief and charitable organizations to unite and raise donations abroad so that the collected donations can be distributed by the committee for emergency relief.

It is also heard that the committee has received a reply telegram from Zhu Qinglan in Beiping, informing them that he will go south in the near future to jointly discuss and implement the plan.

Representatives have been appointed to petition the central government. Excerpts of relevant news are as follows:

Appointment of Representatives to Petition in Beijing: The business community believes that since this city resolved to boycott Japanese goods, various regions have responded actively and have organized anti-Japanese and aid-to-overseas-Chinese organizations to implement economic severance with Japan. However, the actions of the masses must be led by the party headquarters in order to achieve twice the result with half the effort. It has been decided to appoint Wang Xiaolai, Wang Jie'an, Chen Songyuan, Zhang Minghai, and other four people as representatives to petition the central party headquarters in Beijing to issue an order for party headquarters and mass organizations in all regions to rise up together to boycott Japanese goods.

Stores Should Mark the Source of Goods: The Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday issued a notice to all industries in the city stating that according to a letter from the Anti-Japanese Association, the goods sold in the stores of various industries in this city often do not indicate their source, making it difficult to identify which goods are Japanese and which are domestic. This is inconvenient for customers who purchase goods and creates many obstacles for the association's inspections. Therefore, the tenth standing committee meeting resolved to notify all stores to clearly mark the source of goods within ten days. Please ask the association to send personnel to investigate in order to prevent counterfeiting. It is hereby requested that this be investigated and transferred to the industry guilds to notify the affiliated stores to comply. We deeply anticipate this. It is hoped that this will be investigated and transferred for compliance.

Registration of Goods to Be Handled in Accordance with Regulations: The Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday replied to the Sugar Industry Association regarding the registration of Japanese goods to be handled in accordance with regulations. The letter states: "Dear Sirs, We received your letter on the 14th of this month regarding the goods of Yuantaiheng Sugar Company that were seized. You stated that they had previously declared their willingness to pay relief funds and supplement the registration. However, it has been more than ten days since we requested information from your association on how this matter is being handled, but we have not received a reply. We have already replied to your association's letter of July 31 stating that for registration, a registration form should first be obtained and filled out in accordance with the regulations, and then transferred to the Anti-Japanese Association for handling in accordance with the regulations. We believe that you have read it. Subsequently, on August 4, we sent another letter to the Anti-Japanese Association stating that the goods seized by the company were indeed registered with the association on August 1 and requested that they be handled in accordance with the regulations after the registration period expired. The association replied that they would handle it in accordance with the regulations after the forms were sent. This is the course of this case. As for how the Anti-Japanese Association handled it later, since there are already steps to deal with Japanese goods in such cases, which can be based on the above, it has been stated that we will not reply to each case. This is the reason for your association's request. However, the meaning of 'handling in accordance with regulations' in your association's so-called request to transfer to the Anti-Japanese Association for handling in accordance with regulations seems to refer to immediately approving its passage and sale. However, the procedures in this regard are not simple. After the association receives the tables sent by us, the first step is to review or investigate, the second step is to inspect and add seals, and the third step is to obtain a certificate for sale. The goods registered by each industry are thousands upon thousands, and they must be handled one by one. Before this procedure is completed by the association, it is naturally impossible to inform you. This is a detailed letter in reply for your investigation and transmission to the Shanghai Sugar Industry Association."

West Kitchen Workers Went on Strike the Day Before Yesterday Afternoon 140

Due to Assistance with Negotiations on Treatment Conditions for Western Restaurant Workers

Following the refusal of employers to reinstate Western restaurant workers in this city who had resumed work on the orders of the authorities the day before yesterday more than one hundred Western kitchen workers joined the strike on the evening of the previous day to offer their support and the negotiations on their treatment conditions have also begun. The situation yesterday is recorded below in separate sections:

West Kitchen Strike: The Western restaurant industry is divided into two sections: one is the waiters, belonging to the Western Restaurant Workers' Union; the other is the head cooks, belonging to the West Kitchen Workers' Union. The workers of the Western Restaurant Workers' Union went on strike collectively over treatment conditions. After the employers refused to reinstate them when they resumed work on orders the day before yesterday the West Kitchen Workers' Union, to show their support, joined the strike uniformly at 6 p.m. on the afternoon of the previous day (the 15th). To maintain business, restaurants such as Quanjiafu, Daguanlou, Xinlicha, Taipingyang, Zuihechun, and Huangong were maintained by the managers who personally worked to ensure they could continue to operate normally.

Union Congress: The Western Restaurant Workers' Union held a meeting of member representatives at 3 p.m. yesterday, attended by over a hundred people. Wu Shenxiang was elected as chairman. He reported on the refusal of the employers to reinstate the workers after they had resumed work on orders from above, as well as the situation of the West Kitchen Workers' Union joining the strike. Following this, discussions began and resolutions were passed: (1) to submit a further request to the City Party Department and the Social Affairs Bureau to punish the employers who refused to reinstate the workers; (2) to send representatives to various restaurants to persuade non-union members who continued to work and disrupt the strike discipline.

Beginning of Negotiations: The Social Affairs Bureau had summoned parties for questioning in order to facilitate mediation regarding the treatment conditions put forward by the Western Restaurant Workers' Union, but due to the absence of the employers, progress could not be made. From yesterday, the West Kitchen Workers' Union dispatched representatives to act as mediators and the Western Restaurant Industry Association also dispatched representatives to begin negotiations with the workers' side. A resolution may be reached within days.

Union Statement: The Shanghai Western Restaurant Trade Workers' Union refutes the statement of the Trade Association and informs all circles of the truth, writing: "Fellow elders, brothers, and comrades across the country! This spontaneous strike by Western restaurant workers is because the managers of various Western restaurants intentionally sabotage the labor movement, and have no sincerity in accepting the treatment terms we have proposed. They even dare to dismiss workers one by one in labor disputes, thereby arousing the public outrage of all workers. Know that the dark secrets of what these managers do is to deceive the true capitalists above, and oppress and exploit the workers below. However, our proposed improvement terms do not cause any loss to the capitalists, but merely aim to reclaim the various rights that have been gradually stripped away from us by the managers, and to correct the illegal means of arbitrary dismissal of workers, and to break the reason why petty cash is not made public." Because the income of our workers is only three or four yuan per month, we rely entirely on adding petty cash and extra foreign dollars. Unexpectedly, this petty cash is not only not distributed publicly as usual, but is over-collected and under-reported, and then ingenious names are used, such as Taiping shares, Caishen shares, and public accumulation shares, etc., but in fact, they are all pocketed by the managers. The illegal organized Trade Association in 1927 also has its expenses drawn from petty cash, extracting one share from each shop every month, and accumulating to seven or eight thousand yuan so far, excluding expenses. Even more outrageous is that workers who do not work in the shop also have this petty cash extracted for miscellaneous expenses such as laundry, flowers, tea, uniforms, passenger ticket stationery, etc., also extracted from this petty cash. Managers already get huge salaries and rebates for purchasing goods, as well as rewards and dividends from the capitalists, which are considerable. As for us wanting to limit him to no more than three shares, one is to uphold magnanimity, and the other is to prevent them from asking for whatever they want. If the manager deprives this reward, the workers serve customers like slaves. Since the manager's personality is high, so-called hospitality to customers in person, etc., his labor is an obligation that should be fulfilled on his position, how can he shirk the duty of being in the service and say he deserves to be paid. If he is not worthy, it is still difficult to share, not to wait for the workers to demand improvement. There are already examples of similar words wanting to cover up the eyes and ears of the world, and the fifth and sixth articles say they are violating the law. For example, in the third article, the union's expenses and the expenses for the undertakings to be handled should be appropriately subsidized by the capitalists according to the union law. We require extracting one share of petty cash, which originally belongs to the workers. It is nothing more than adding a procedure to them through their hands. If the fifth article is to limit the apprentices with specific regulations, such as the sixth article, workers should not be dismissed without reason, and workers who do not join the union should be used to obstruct the union and labor movement, and in the future, workers should be dismissed according to the general rules of the union. Ask, do these requirements violate the law? Such as the fourth article, double wages are required in July and August because the Western restaurant business is particularly good in July and August. The workers' work is either all night or all day, and their hard work is doubled. All labor festival commemorative festivals should be on leave, and those who do not stop work should also be paid double wages. This kind of requirement is perfectly reasonable. If the seventh article says that the kitchen waste is related to the capital of the shop owner, how can it be said that it is usually put into the petty vendors' public distribution? It is obvious that there is a contradiction and shield in the language. Because the kitchen staff has no unexpected income other than wages and petty cash, this kind of waste should belong to them to enjoy. Moreover, the level of living is increasing day by day. Our workers cannot only not improve their living and improve their treatment, but also be exploited layer by layer, still being bound by these fierce and vicious managers like cattle and horses, wouldn't they be crying miserably? They intentionally cite new workers to refuse the reinstatement of our workers, which aroused the public outrage of all the Western kitchen workers in Shanghai, and they all went on strike to show their support and to urge them to wake up. From now on, stand together, endure the pain, and strive to fight a desperate battle with these demons until the purpose of signing a contract in good faith is achieved. I also hope that all circles will understand the truth and uphold our justice."
