Appeals from All Walks of Life for Flood Relief 142

Governor Zhang's Telegram on Behalf of Disaster Victims in Northern Jiangsu Begging for Assistance Reads:

Urgent: Shanghai Flood Relief Associations in Various Provinces: Public Announcement. Unfortunately, the country has suffered repeated disasters. The devastation caused by this flood is unprecedented. Taking Northern Jiangsu as an example, the floodwaters in the Gaoyou and Shaobo areas are vast and boundless. From Shaobo and above to Qingjiang along the west bank of the river, the entire area is a vast expanse, completely turned into a swamp. Houses have collapsed, the old and weak have drowned, and the number is uncountable. Those who have not drowned and have escaped are living in sheds on the west bank of the river, stretching for hundreds of miles, all being grass sheds for disaster victims. Wives lead their husbands, children carry their mothers, emaciated and haggard, crying for food and clothing. White-haired old people and yellow-mouthed infants groan on the roadside, and grieving women and orphans wail on both banks. The sight of the disaster-stricken people is unbearable to witness. The Wuliba and Lujin towns east of Gaoyou have recently collapsed one after another. The disaster victims along the east bank of the river are displaced and have nowhere to live. The desolate situation is beyond words. As the Governor of Jiangsu, I have witnessed this tragic situation and am worried day and night. I humbly request that your associations provide urgent assistance so that these remaining people will not be left to die. It would be a great blessing for the region and the country. Zhang Zhijiang humbly awaits orders with urgency. [Seal]

The Ningbo Fellow Townsmen Association in Shanghai Received a Letter Yesterday from the Zhengyang Town Chamber of Commerce and Various Trade Associations in Shou County, Anhui, stating:

Respectfully, Zhengyang is located in a low-lying area and is prone to flooding, especially this year's flood, which is unprecedented. Since the beginning of summer, continuous rain has formed a swamp. Following the wheat harvest, torrential rain fell for three days and nights, and the nearby dikes were all submerged. Crops were all swept away by the flood, and countless people and livestock drowned. At that time, the water from the upper reaches of the Huai and Pi Rivers surged and combined with the rivers in the lower reaches, such as the Fei and Ying Rivers, which were blocked and unable to drain away, causing the water level to continue to rise, becoming a vast ocean. Zhengyang was in danger, with many parts of the city walls collapsed, the streets three to four feet deep, shops closed and sealed, boats passing through the main streets and alleys, and residents' houses collapsing. Those who came from afar to escape bandits and those who came from nearby because of the flood either gathered in temples or stayed in high buildings in the city, and some were trapped on sandbars, clinging to tree branches and calling for help, living in desolate tombs and neighboring wild ghosts, and the dry coffins floated into the city with the waves, and the floating corpses roamed with the waves. Passersby grieved for their fish, and residents were all in Chen's distress. Women and children wailed, and the old and weak awaited death. The water soaked and exposed them, their bodies were swollen and unbearable, and their faces were emaciated. The Rakshasas of hell appeared, and the tragic situation was like this. Even if Zheng Xia presented a map, he could not have painted it in such detail. Our association witnessed this and was heartbroken. We have reported the disaster situation to the Nanjing Central Disaster Relief Committee and the Anhui Provincial Government for their review. However, the water tide is about to recede, and we all hope for sunny days. On July 24th and 25th, there was another heavy rain, and the flood tide rose sharply, which was even worse than the previous days. The vast catastrophe has been repeatedly encountered, and we lament that the lives of the remaining people are completely cut off. We have always admired your association's sincere feelings for your hometown and your concern for the suffering of the people. We hereby inform you of the serious water disaster in Zhengyang and the situation of lives being on the verge of death. We humbly request that you publish it in the newspaper and appeal on our behalf. If you can send national currency as soon as possible to obtain relief funds, or if you can accept donations from philanthropists, you will be bathing in compassion. This is all bestowed by your association. We respectfully kowtow on behalf of the disaster victims, and so on. We replied by letter that we would cooperate in calling for assistance.

Pan Gongzhan Speaks on Nationalism and Anti-Japanese Movement 145

Broadcast on the Great China Radio Station Yesterday

The Guomin Society said that the Third District Party Department of this city invited Mr. Pan Gongzhan, a member of the Standing Committee of the City Party Department and Director of the City Social Affairs Bureau, to broadcast a speech entitled "Nationalism and the Anti-Japanese Movement" at the wireless broadcasting station of the Dachanghua Electrical Appliance Company on Nanjing Road at 10 a.m. yesterday (the 16th). The following is a record of his speech: "Everyone, today I am here to speak on nationalism and the Anti-Japanese Movement. Nationalism is the first of the Three Principles of the People of the Chinese Kuomintang. There are three main points of nationalism. The first point is to treat the five major ethnic groups of China, Han, Manchu, Mongolian, Hui, and Tibetan, equally. The second point is to treat all ethnic groups in the world equally. The third point is to help all small and weak ethnic groups in the world so that they are in an equal position. Combining these three meanings can make nationalism achieve its completion. Nationalism is to prevent any ethnic group from being oppressed by any ethnic group or oppressing any ethnic group. It is to put the Chinese nation on an equal footing with other nations in the world. Now, the imperialists are using military and economic forces to invade China, which is caused by unequal treaties. This time, Japan instigated Koreans to massacre Chinese overseas Chinese, resulting in numerous casualties and property losses. Why should Chinese people in Korea be slaughtered by Koreans? The cause is extremely small. The Japanese transplanted Koreans to my Jilin Wanbaoshan to forcibly plant Chinese farmers' fields, and conflicts occurred. Japan immediately sent troops to protect the Koreans and forcibly seize them. This situation is entirely the Japanese using the Koreans to invade my country. After the Sino-Japanese War of Jiawu, Korea has become a colony of Japan. Since then, Korea has no country. Therefore, the Japanese will never want Korea to develop. Why does Japan want to help the Koreans to forcibly seize our farmland? This is Japan's clever way to use the Koreans to colonize the three eastern provinces. In case the Chinese people oppose, they will send troops to interfere. Because of the Wanbaoshan case, Japan provoked Chinese and Korean animosity. The Koreans relied on the Japanese army and slaughtered my Chinese overseas Chinese. This is what Japan wants. Japan treats China as an insignificant country and can do whatever it wants. This situation is completely contrary to the nationalism advocated by Sun Yat-sen. If we all believe in nationalism, we should all unite to resist Japan's aggressive behavior. Japanese warlords and Japanese hooligans do not want the Chinese nation to have a position in the world. Under this kind of oppression, we should all uphold the same goal to resist Japan. Now we must pay attention to the methods of anti-Japanese. Thinking of this, we must look at the attitude taken by the government and the people. We should be willing to forgive the government because there are bandits in the country in Jiangxi, Fujian, Hunan, and other provinces. In the north, there is the rebellion of Shi Yousan. In Guangdong, there is the reaction of unscrupulous politicians. The losses from floods in various provinces exceed 80 million to 100 million. In such a position, the government must suppress bandits on one hand, fight rebels on the other hand, deal with unscrupulous politicians in Guangdong on the other hand, and provide relief to the floods in various provinces on the other hand. How much energy can be devoted to diplomacy? Therefore, to make diplomacy strong, we should look at the backing of diplomacy. Now, the Chinese army is not substantial and has no power to resist Japan. Therefore, now we can only fight with justice and the people's own power to make the Japanese people at home automatically realize and oppose the Japanese warlords and hooligans. Chinese people have boycotted Japanese goods several times, but they have failed in the end. Why do we have to do it again this time? There are two points worth noting in this anti-Japanese movement. The first point is that we hope that it is not only for the Korean incident that we oppose Japan, but to recognize that our Chinese nation demands a way out and opposes Japan, and the anti-Japanese work cannot be stopped just because the Korean case is over. The second point is that we hope that the anti-Japanese movement will be planned, not a general anti-Japanese movement. China now has its own raw materials for most of its goods, and most of the manufactured goods are foreign. According to China's customs statistics for the past two years, six out of ten of these goods are Japanese goods. If China continues like this, it will become a slave of Japan. Looking at it this way, we must have a plan to boycott Japanese goods and revitalize domestic goods. For example, although China has a lot of coal reserves, it does not have enough power to supply factories across the country. Then, the factories can only use Japanese coal. There is also a layer to boycott Japanese goods. First, we must boycott luxury goods, and daily necessities and raw materials cannot be forced to boycott. Finally, we hope that we will not boycott Japanese goods and use other foreign goods. If we cannot achieve these points, the five-point fever will only be ridiculed by the Japanese. However, the biggest key lies in the hands of the business community. It is like seeking skin from a tiger to discuss boycotting Japanese goods with the business community. When the business community starts to boycott Japanese goods, they must first ask whether to inspect and whether to seize the goods. If merchants are willing to boycott automatically, there is no need to ask whether to inspect or whether to seize the goods. These two sentences can already prove that the merchants do not sincerely boycott Japanese goods. Before the Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Association started inspecting Japanese goods, the Japanese goods piled up in the Shanghai warehouses had already been taken away. Many people say that merchants do not talk about nationalism and only know how to make personal fortunes. This kind of criticism cannot be said to be completely wrong. Now, we can only earnestly advise the business community to discover their conscience and not sell or transport Japanese goods automatically, then the boycott will be effective. It is not effective to force merchants to boycott. If there is a boycott plan, after five or ten years, Japanese goods will naturally be eliminated without boycott.

The Pudong Procuratorate Seized Japanese Goods 146

Those Who Protect Unscrupulous Merchants Will Be Punished

The Pudong Procuratorate of the Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Committee found more than 3,000 packages of Japanese goods, potato flour, also known as Dong Sheng flour, in the Yuanlai Warehouse, Lujia Ferry, Pudong on the 15th of this month. It immediately reported it to the Investigation Section of the committee and intended to detain it. After the Investigation Section forwarded it, it immediately sent two specialists to the warehouse to verify that it was Japanese goods. Then, the Investigation Section ordered the district to detain all 3,000 packages of the goods and intended to transfer the goods to the Gongda Warehouse for storage at about 6 pm. Suddenly, a certain Shao came out to interfere, claiming to be a member of the Anti-Japanese Association, intending to protect unscrupulous merchants and prevent transportation, and uttered insulting words and scolded the inspectors. The situation was turbulent and unreasonable. Later, the inspector found out that there was no Shao in the executive committee of the Anti-Japanese Association. He was obviously posing as a swindler, so he immediately added a painful rebuke and intended to detain him for handling. The certain Shao knew that he was in the wrong, so he begged again and again and was willing to hand over the obstruction process in writing to the office for forwarding to the Anti-Japanese Association for discussion. At that time, the office allowed the request because the certain Shao was the person in charge of a certain trade association and urged all the inspectors to continue to transfer the goods to the Gongda Warehouse. At the same time, it reported the case process to the Anti-Japanese Association for verification. It is heard that the Anti-Japanese Association intends to submit it to the Executive Committee for discussion and give the certain Shao a serious punishment to deter wrongdoers.

Progress of the Automatic Establishment of a Fine Yarn Factory 148

Talk by Xie Weiqing, Director of Preparation

Since the knitting industry in this city advocated the policy of automatically establishing a fine yarn factory and implementing the policy of goods for goods, it has been deeply sympathized by all parties and the progress has been extremely smooth. According to Xie Weiqing, director of the fine yarn factory preparation, it is imperative for our country to establish a fine yarn factory at present. I personally went to Europe and the United States last year to conduct on-the-spot investigations. The most advanced textile machinery is in the UK. In the future, the fine yarn factory in our industry should also carefully select purchases. The factory established by our industry will tentatively set the capital at one million taels at the beginning of its establishment, and then plan to expand it after it is successfully run. I have prepared a detailed plan and submitted it to the trade association for discussion. Since the establishment of the fine yarn factory preparation office, the subscriptions have been very enthusiastic, which proves the urgent need. It is heard that the number of confirmed subscribers has reached more than 300,000 taels. Jardine Matheson & Co. Telegraphed Enquiring About the Whereabouts of the Kuang Sang Steamer 150

News After the Weisen Steamer Ran Aground Yesterday

The Continental Daily reported that Jardine Matheson & Co.'s Kuang Sang Steamer sailed from Shanghai to Shantou and Hong Kong at 4 pm on the 8th of this month. It has been seven days since then and there has been no news. The company's ship, together with the British warship, searched along the way and found no trace. It is expected that it encountered strong winds on Sunday night and either had an accident or drifted to a remote beach with no way to communicate with the outside world. The ship was carrying 2,900 tons of cargo and had 50 crew members. The number of passengers is unknown because the tickets were sold by the compradors. The ship was 2,283 tons and was built in 1902.

It was also reported that after the company's Weisen Steamer ran aground in Nanguan, news was received yesterday that the hull had tilted and there was a danger of cracking. There are still several crew members on board. The Fuson has already loaded food and went to provide relief and search for Kuang Sang along the way.

Shanghai Shipping Merchants Petition for Exemption from Zhejiang Province Water Conservancy Expenses 151

The Shanghai Shipping Association recently sent telegrams to the Civil Affairs Department and Construction Department of the Zhejiang Provincial Government stating that, according to a joint statement from member shipping companies operating in Zhejiang, the Zhejiang Construction Department proposed levying a surtax of 10% on all provincial steamboat, passenger ship, and cargo tickets to be used as water conservancy funds for various districts. This proposal was approved by the Zhejiang Provincial Government and circulated to various city and county governments with a public notice announcing implementation starting August 1st. All shipping merchants, upon receiving this order, were greatly surprised. It was noted that the shipping business has been declining in recent years. Due to the exchange rate with the gold pound, the prices of various materials have skyrocketed. In addition, rice prices are high, and crew wages and food expenses have increased many times over the past. In terms of income, the industry has been affected by foreign ships and trucking, not only preventing any increase but also causing a daily decline. This environment has left the industry in a precarious situation, on the verge of collapse, with hardships difficult to describe in detail. Fortunately, the provisional constitution stipulates that private shipping businesses should be encouraged and protected. It is hoped that the government will abide by these provisions and provide as much support as possible for development. However, the Zhejiang Provincial Construction Department, after ceasing the collection of "Zhenjuan" donations, issued an order for private shipping businesses to collect a 10% surtax for water conservancy funds, without specifying a time limit, which has aroused public concerns. The Zhejiang Provincial Government believes that the surtax is collected from passengers and merchants, and that shipping merchants are merely collecting agents, which will not affect their business. This is due to a lack of understanding of the commercial situation and a failure to consider the facts. The steamboat business in Zhejiang Province is already like a spent arrow, with cargo and passenger traffic declining daily. If passengers and merchants are forced to pay the surtax, they will inevitably look elsewhere, either abandoning us for others or abandoning boats for land. Even a meager attempt to survive will be impossible, and the impact on the shipping industry will be significant. Moreover, water conservancy is a local public service and should be funded by local areas. It is unfair to solely burden passengers. Furthermore, this surtax is not stipulated by central laws and regulations, and shipping merchants are not collection agencies, making it inconvenient to collect. If passengers are unwilling to pay, how will they cope? Therefore, it is truly difficult to collect the surtax. Based on the above reasons and facts, all shipping merchants find it impossible to comply with the Zhejiang Provincial Government's decision to order merchant ships to collect a 10% surtax for water conservancy funds. It is requested that the association telegraph for its cancellation to maintain the shipping industry. The association has reviewed the above and found the statements to be factual and reasonable. Therefore, we urgently appeal, humbly requesting your understanding and approval for cancellation, so as to allow the industry to survive. We await your orders with apprehension.

Respectfully,

Yu Hede, Chairman of the Shanghai Shipping Association

Memorial Service for Gu Jingen and Dai Tingzu 153

Held at the Tianhou Palace Yesterday

The Shanghai Municipal People's Memorial Service for Gu Jingen and Dai Tingzu, who were harmed by American sailors, was held at the Tianhou Palace at 10:00 AM yesterday. Participants included more than 100 organizations such as the City Chamber of Commerce, the City People's Federation, the Postal and Publishing Industry Union, the Cigarette Industry Union, Fujian and Anhui Native Place Associations, the Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Committee, and representatives from the Municipal Party Headquarters, including Mao Yun, totaling several thousand people. Details of the meeting are as follows:

Meeting Staff: Chief Celebrant: Zhang Xianfang; Chief Administrators: Zhu Xuefan, Li Yongxiang, Gong Yuting, Wang Yongliang, Zhao Shusheng, Long Peiyun; Master of Ceremonies: Chen Peide

Meeting Order: (1) Play mournful music; (2) All stand at attention; (3) Sing the party song; (4) Pay three respects to the portrait of Sun Yat-sen and the spirit tablets of Gu Jingen and Dai Tingzu; (5) Respectfully read Sun Yat-sen's last will; (6) Observe a moment of silence for mourning; (7) Present flowers; (8) Read the memorial oration; (9) Report; (10) Speeches; (11) Family representatives deliver reply; (12) Play mournful music; (13) Adjourn

The memorial oration of the meeting was proclaimed by head administrator Zhao Xie Sheng, then the Shanghai Municipal Representatives of All Circles on the Sixteenth Day of August, Republic of China the Twentieth Year, respectfully with incense and flowers offer their homage before the Spirits of the two Gentlemen Gu Jing Gen and Dai Tingzu, and link it with the following expression: Alas, the Ling Mountains are blue-green, the rivers and seas vast and boundless, heroic men are cut short, and justice is lost. Heaven is desolate, the earth is gloomy, all who are Chinese-stomached, who does not feel the pain! Alas, those foreign races, eyeing like tigers. The two gentlemen unfortunately bore their brunt, contending in the drinking of bullets at Xiepu [Whangpoo river], with repeated negotiations, a stance of taking advantage due to dragging things along. Still! Glorious China, well-dressed and capped, only we patriots eliminate the reeking smell. Of one accord and one heart, defend the nation and preserve the race; from beginning to end, follow the principle. To take revenge and wipe out disgrace, pledge an oath to be heroic. The two gentlemen's souls, in the spring soil have glory, may your spirits not be obscured, but come to us, come and partake! Alas, how lofty the sound.

The report speech was delivered by the Shanghai Municipal All Circles Anti-US Sailors Brutal Acts Committee representative Zhu Xuefan, and the Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Committee representative Li Yongxiang, reporting on the victims’ Gu and Dai’s account of how their harm occurred and the negotiation progress. The guidance words were delivered by the city party department representative and each sector’s representatives Wang Yongliang, Gong Yuting, Weng Ruifu, Lu Muqin, Ge Yunting and others, successively giving speeches with extremely melancholy sentiments.

Family Thank You Speech: Gu Jingen's wife led her children to the meeting, her appearance distraught, seemingly unable to bear her grief, which moved all who watched. Finally, Gu Jingen's younger brother, Gu Awu, delivered a thank-you speech. Mournful music was played, and the meeting adjourned.

Rice Boat Runs Aground in Southern Huangpu River 159

A self-selling rice boat owned by Tao Bosheng from Pudong recently purchased more than 200 dan [unit of dry measure] of rice in the Songjiang area. Seeing that the Shanghai market had slightly recovered, he rushed to Shanghai to sell it as soon as possible. Unexpectedly, a gale broke out a few days ago. Tao's boat, loaded with rice, was anchored in the Southern Huangpu River for two days, but the wind did not subside. Tao became extremely anxious, fearing a loss in price. He ordered his crew to set sail. However, the boat ran aground on a sandbar in the Tagang area of the Southern Huangpu River due to the strong wind the previous morning. All six people on board fell into the water. Four of them were rescued by fishing boats. Tao's father and another crew member are missing, presumably drowned. The capsized boat is now lying sideways on the beach. The rice on board was washed away by the wind and waves, leaving only the hull. The loss of the boat and rice is estimated at five to six thousand yuan. Moreover, Tao's father and the other crew member are presumed dead, causing Tao great distress. Yesterday, he hired a boat to salvage the boat and search for the bodies of his father and crew member.

The District Court Will Be Open All Day 160

Starting Today

The Shanghai District Court has a summer vacation every year from July 1st to the end of August. During this two-month period, its office hours are from 8:00 AM to 12:00 PM. However, in case of emergencies, a clerk on duty will handle them. This year, the summer vacation was also followed as usual. However, before it was fifteen days before the end, an order was received from the ministry stating that this year is not hot and all departments and their subordinate agencies do not have summer vacations and orders were made to change office hours. After receiving the order, the court has now changed its office hours to 8:00 AM to 12:00 PM and 2:00 PM to 4:00 PM, starting today (the 17th).

Inspection of Male Corpses and Notes by the District Court 162

Recently, the Shanghai District Court has received reports from local guarantors regarding the examination of several cases of unidentified male corpses who were assassinated. Therefore, the procuratorate has ordered the arrest of the murderers and an investigation to identify the relatives to claim the bodies. (1) In front of the Pingjiang Public Hall, there was a male corpse, about twenty years old, naked from the waist up and wearing shorts. The throat and head had knife wounds. (2) Near the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway on Xiaoshadu, there was a male corpse, about thirty years old, wearing a white cloth short shirt. The hands and feet had knife wounds. (3) Inside Jinkang Lane, Xiaodongmen, there was a male corpse in a hanging position. Examination revealed that it was a case of relocation of the corpse after injury to the back of the head. The corpse was about thirty years old and wearing black shorts and a shirt. (4) A male corpse was recovered from the Yangshupu River. The hands and feet were tied behind the back. Examination revealed that the corpse was about thirty years old, wearing a white cloth shirt, white cloth trousers, and leather shoes. It was determined that he was drowned by bandits. None of the above cases have been claimed by relatives. Therefore, the police have been dispatched to investigate relatives to provide them with the body and to begin the investigation. At the same time, Chief Xu of the police was instructed to arrest the murderers and bring them to justice.

Qian Yunhe's Painting Exhibition Moved 165

The painting exhibition of the famous painter Qian Yunhe, formerly known as "Sick Crane," was originally held at the New World Printing Company on Wangping Street, but the space was too small to display all the works. Starting on the 16th, the exhibition was moved to the third floor of the New World Hotel, where all the works were displayed. Minutes of the Standing Committee of the Hongshun Mutual Aid Society 167

The Hongshun Mutual Aid Society held its tenth regular meeting of directors and supervisors yesterday, with 26 attendees. Chairman Yang Wendao conducted the meeting with customary formalities. After the report, the following matters were discussed: (1) The number of new members joining the association has been increasing. In addition to those who have registered in accordance with the regulations, there are also those who have been registered by introducers for a long time but have not attended the meetings, even after notification. How should this be handled? It was resolved to send personnel to investigate the truth. If it is due to delays or relocation abroad, their names will be retained. If the addresses are not accurate or there are other reasons, the investigation will verify the situation and distinguish between retention and deletion to avoid having vacancies. (2) Tang Jianting of the Relief Section reported that the condolence money from the Funeral Department is originally intended to relieve urgent needs. Once the person in charge reports to the association, the full amount is immediately disbursed, and personnel are dispatched to escort the coffin on the day of the funeral to express condolences. However, the subsequent collection of condolence money has not been submitted in accordance with the regulations, which is a serious matter for the future of the association. It was resolved to publish a notice to all members that it is their obligation to fulfill their obligations to the Mutual Aid Society. When collecting condolence money, they should submit it to the Funeral Department within one week to maintain financial stability and facilitate the work. (3) During the seventh meeting of the former group leader, Liu Quangen proposed to raise donations to relieve flood victims and overseas Chinese affected by the Wanbaoshan incident. The matter was submitted to the directors and supervisors for deliberation and implementation. It was resolved that the flood disaster in various provinces and cities is severe, and the victims are suffering innocently. The association will notify all members to make donations, and members will voluntarily solicit donations. The matter will be submitted to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau for the record and will be implemented. It is also planned to have the martial arts actors from the Sports Department donate some of their skills to raise funds, which will be turned over to various relief associations for distribution to express the enthusiasm of the entire association. The rest was omitted. The meeting adjourned.

How should this be handled? Resolved: to report the situation to the Municipal Social Bureau for a decision. Passed. (2) How to self-govern against the manager's arbitrary wage deductions? To report the situation to the Municipal People's Training Committee for record and to organize a labor union to seek liberation. Passed by all. (3) The Municipal Social Bureau sent personnel on the 14th to investigate the labor-management situation. Pending the authorities' orders, representatives will be nominated for negotiation. Resolved: to nominate Zhang Yulin and others to be responsible for the process. Passed. (4) All workers should be vigilant against reactionary elements undermining the workers' organization during the organization period. Resolved: passed.

The Duck Slaughtering Industry Labor Union held its third board meeting yesterday. Chairman Sun Panfu. Matters for discussion: (1) The union's income and expenditure accounts should be promptly announced and distributed to all members to avoid suspicion. Resolved: passed. (2) Member Zhang Tiansheng and others have resisted paying monthly fees, and warnings have been ineffective. How should this be handled? Resolved: to report to the Municipal Party Department for review. (3) All workers are requesting to revise the contract due to difficult living conditions. The five most important clauses should be proposed. Resolved: passed. (4) Nominate Sun Panfu, Ruan Changqing, Yu Axu, Jiang Ade, and Jiang Liangcai as attending representatives. Resolved: passed. (5) The relocation of the union headquarters to 67 Youche Wharf, rented by Ruan Changqing, should be ratified. Resolved: approved for ratification.

The Military Uniform Industry Labor Union held its ninth board meeting yesterday. Chairman Yu Zhixun. Key resolutions: (1) Member Ren Hengzu privately lent his membership certificate. His membership should be revoked. If he can repent and reform, he will be allowed to rejoin. (2) Worker Yu A'lai impersonated a member to work. A fine of five yuan should be imposed, and he should be ordered to formally join the union. (3) In the future, if anyone loses their membership certificate and requests a replacement, machinists should pay an additional membership and certificate fee of one yuan and two jiao, and tailors should pay an additional fee of one yuan and six jiao. The lost certificate number should be published in the newspaper to declare it void. (4) All members who joined during the preparatory period and have not yet paid their membership fees should be treated the same as new members. The Investigation Section should work with the Guidance Section to collect the outstanding fees by the end of this month. Those who fail to pay by the deadline will have their membership revoked.

The Dock Workers' Reorganization Committee held its 88th regular meeting the day before yesterday. Chairman Shen Wenyuan opened the meeting with due ceremony and reported. (1) The Third Branch of the Fourth District reported that worker badges should be issued by name. If jobless hooligans disrupt work, they request proper protection. (2) (Omitted). (3) Committee member Liu Defu has been on leave for nearly two months without returning. How should this be handled? Resolved: all living expenses for the two months of leave will not be paid.

The Fragrance Industry Labor Union held its fourth board meeting the day before yesterday. Local News 2

Completion of Automated Telephone Lines on Route Pichon and Route Hweisan 170

New Lines in Use Since Yesterday

The Shanghai Telephone Company's construction of automated telephone exchanges in the Route Pichon and Route Hweisan districts has been completed simultaneously. All 3,400 subscribers in the Route Pichon district and 1,900 subscribers in the Route Hweisan district were switched to automated telephone service after midnight on the 15th. This eliminates the inconvenience of calling for an operator. The conversion of telephones to automated service in Shanghai has taken another step forward.

Reception for the Press The Shanghai Telephone Company's new exchanges on Route Pichon and Route Hweisan were switched to new lines at 1:00 AM on the 16th. The company gave a reception for the press at the new exchange on Route Pichon at 2:00 PM on the 13th, where staff member Fan Ningshou accompanied them on a tour of the various departments: (1) The basement is the entry point for the ground lines. (2) The testing room can immediately calculate the location of an obstacle if an obstacle occurs, or it can emit a sound to remind users to return the handset to the machine if they forget to do so. (3) The power room uses AC electricity from an electric power plant and transforms it into 48-volt DC electricity. (4) The battery room uses stored electricity to continue generating electricity when an external power interruption occurs. (5) The air conditioning room is specifically designed to regulate temperature to keep each part warm in winter and cool in summer and to protect the equipment. (6) The switching room upstairs is currently being prepared for line changes. The procedure on the night of the 15th only took a few seconds.

Converting Line Heads The procedure for converting manual switchboard telephones to automated telephones is extremely burdensome, more than doubling the difficulty of installing new telephones. Therefore, the company has been preparing for several months. Even for the overnight switch of the switchboards and conversion of line heads, a detailed work procedure was prepared in advance, with a detailed allocation of the duties of each employee and the order of their work, totaling 82 pages. This shows the complexity of the procedure and the thoroughness of the arrangement. On the evening of the day before yesterday, all employees gathered at the old and new exchange districts and went to their designated work locations to complete the final preparations. Then, they quietly waited for the arrival of 1:00 AM. At 12:45 AM, the engineering manager issued a preparation order at the Hweisan exchange, and all employees were ready to go, holding their tools in hand. Then, the bells rang, and the scheduled time had arrived. The manager gave an order, and all personnel began work simultaneously, first cutting off the old lines and then connecting to the new machines. Before long, the conversion was completed, and testing work was then performed. If any minor shortcomings were found, their location was immediately identified and corrected. It was reported that the testing work continued throughout yesterday to ensure perfection.

Condition of the New Exchange The entrance to the new exchange is the power room, which is equipped with a generator, a power distribution machine, and numerous batteries to generate and regulate the current required for the telephones in the area. Next is the testing room, where all trunk cables leading to various areas and branch cables connecting to subscribers in the area enter the room from the ground and are connected to a distribution frame, from which they are distributed to the various parts of the switchboard. There are several trunk cables, each containing as many as 2,224 telephone lines, which are large and substantial. The distribution frame is equipped with fuses to prevent the switchboard from burning out if the telephone line comes into contact with lightning or power lines. It is said that subscribers also have similar fuses in their homes to protect their telephones. All of the testing telephone lines and the machinery of the switchboard are installed on the distribution frame and next to the switchboard operator's desk. When a circuit failure occurs, the switchboard operator can immediately detect its location and send a technician to repair it. Further in is the switchboard room, where the automatic switchboards are located, arranged in rows to replace the work of switchboard operators.

Automatic Switching There are tens of thousands of telephones in the foreign concessions. When a subscriber picks up the receiver and rotates the dial, the machine can connect to the called party without fail. Only an extremely ingenious machine can be so accurate and convenient. Readers would probably like to know how it works. When a subscriber picks up the receiver, the line finder on the switchboard starts operating under power and immediately finds the subscriber's line head and connects it to the line selector. At this time, the subscriber can hear a buzzing sound in the receiver, which is called the dial tone. After hearing this tone, the dial can be rotated. The line selector is a machine that automatically selects the required line. Currently, telephone numbers in the concessions have five digits, so there are four sets of line selectors. The first set of line selectors is installed in the exchange in this area and is divided into ten units, each connected to the telephone lines in one area. For example, the first unit is connected to the Central Automatic Telephone Area, the second unit is connected to the Lu Zong Area, the third unit is connected to the West Area, the fourth unit is connected to the North Area, the fifth unit is connected to the Hweisan Area, the sixth unit is connected to the Central Manual Switchboard Area, the seventh unit is connected to the Route Pichon Area, the eighth unit is connected to the Mintini Yin Road Area, the ninth unit is connected to the Fujian Road Area, and the tenth unit is connected to special telephone lines, which have only two digits, such as those used to report alarms to the fire department and the police station. Now, suppose a subscriber in the Hweisan Area wants to call the Route Pichon Area, whose number is "73725." Then, after the subscriber picks up the receiver, the line finder in the Hweisan exchange will immediately connect the subscriber's line head to the line selector and emit a buzzing sound. The subscriber then rotates the dial to the number "7," and the line selector will connect the line to the seventh unit of the first set, thereby connecting to the Route Pichon Area exchange. When the second number "3" is dialed, the second set of line selectors in the Route Pichon Area will connect the line to the "73" branch line. When the third number "7" is dialed again, the third set of machines will connect to the "737" branch line. When the fourth number "2" is dialed again, the fourth set of machines will connect to the "7372" branch line. This branch line has ten pairs of sub-lines. All subscribers whose first four digits are "7372" are connected to this branch line. Finally, when the last digit "5" is dialed, the "73725" telephone line is connected by this branch line. At this time, if no one is talking on the telephone, the bell will ring loudly to call someone to answer the phone. At the same time, the caller will hear a "burr-urr" sound, which indicates that the line has been connected. Conversely, if someone is talking on the line, the caller will hear a "burr-is" sound, which indicates that the line is busy. At this time, the receiver must be hung up, and the call must be made again after a few minutes. When we observe the above-mentioned connection situation, we cannot help but think that if many subscribers call various families with similar numbers at the same time, the switchboard will inevitably feel very crowded. However, according to the actual situation, this concern is unnecessary because the bureau has already taken precautions against this. For example, the Hweisan exchange currently has 3,000 telephone lines and is equipped with 360 line finders, which are connected to 40 line selectors. Moreover, once the connection is established, the line selector can be grounded separately. The average connection time for each line is less than 20 seconds, so there will be no congestion.

Unfinished Work According to people in the company, although the new exchange has been connected and put into use, there is still some unfinished work. During this period, subscribers may experience some difficulty when making calls. First, the new exchange is like a new machine. It is currently in the trial period, so there may inevitably be some things that need to be repaired. Second, the cables and wires in the old exchange still need to be dismantled one by one. At this time, subscribers' telephones may inevitably experience problems. However, the company will do its best to minimize the inconvenience to subscribers.

Rice Prices Fell Again Yesterday 171

Recently, rice prices in Shanghai have been gradually declining. Yesterday, arrivals in Zhabei were very heavy, and demand decreased sharply. According to people in the rice industry, the Social Bureau's order to restore the limit price of 17 yuan within a week is expected to be fulfilled. This is because yesterday, the special polished rice (i.e., the highest quality white rice) had already fallen to 18.7 yuan, 2 jiao less than the current limit price of 18.9 yuan. No. 2 white rice was selling for 17.6 yuan per stone, No. 3 was selling for 17 yuan, foreign xian rice was selling for 16.8 yuan, ke xian rice was selling for 14.8 yuan, inferior rice was selling for 13.4 yuan, and tongbian glutinous rice (i.e., white yuan) was selling for 15.4 yuan, compared to 16.7 yuan in the previous days, a difference of 1.3 yuan.

Homicide Case at the Fasheng New Hotel Solved 172

Bodies of the Two Victims Examined Yesterday The French Police Solved the Case Quickly

At 2:00 PM the day before yesterday, Wang Xiji, who claimed to be from Zhenjiang and wore a white short shirt and pants, went with a friend to Room No. 2 downstairs at the Fasheng New Hotel at 113 Rue Massenet in the French Concession and paid the room fee. He then went out. At 7:00 PM, he returned to the hotel with five friends, entered the room, and closed the door to talk. Twenty minutes later, a burst of gunshots suddenly rang out in the room, about twenty or so. After the gunshots stopped, four people in the room were injured. Wang Xiji, who had come to open the room first, and one other person rushed out the front door and fled south with the three people who had been standing outside the door as lookouts. The hotel then reported to the police station, which sent detectives to take the four injured people by car to the Renji Hospital. Two of them died from their critical injuries before they could be treated. The hospital notified the police station, which sent detectives to the hospital to inquire about the names of the injured. One was named Zhong Ziqing and the other was Chen Yiming. According to Zhong, one of the dead was named Xia Yongsheng and the other was surnamed Xue. The bodies of the two victims were taken to the Tongren Fuyuan Funeral Parlor for examination. The details of the examination were recorded in yesterday's newspaper. However, the identities of the two corpses could not be determined. Yesterday morning, the police station reported to the Second Special District Court and asked Judge Lou Guanxian, forensic doctor Wei Ligong, and clerk Zhao Yifen to come to examine the bodies at 10:00 AM. The names of the two bodies were difficult to distinguish. It was examined that the smaller corpse had four bullet wounds in the right chest, right arm, left leg, and left foot, and the taller corpse had three bullet wounds in the right forehead, left back of the neck, and left side. After clarifying the examination, the judge took his seat, and the detective reported the previous situation and presented the 14 shell casings and two bullets found at the scene of the incident. According to the hotel owner, Wang Jiemei, and the tea server, Zhang Rongsheng, the judge, after verifying the information, declared that Xia Yongsheng and the person surnamed Xue were indeed killed by gunshot wounds and that the murderer was at large and should be arrested and brought to justice by the police. The judge then handed the bodies over to the Tongren Fuyuan Hall for burial. After the examination, the police took photos of the bodies for record purposes. In the afternoon, Xia's wife came to the morgue and identified the shorter body as Xia Yongsheng. The detective in charge of the case then took Xia's wife to the police station for further investigation. It was also learned that after this case occurred, the French police station's special task force detectives, based on what the injured person said about the murderer's address, immediately went out to arrest the suspect, but there were no clues until dawn. At 7:00 AM, an informant reported that the case was committed by Yan Er, a well-known bandit leader from Jiangbei. Yan lived at No. 16 Chongde Fang, Minguo Road, outside the Xiaobeimen, etc. At 7:30 AM, detectives Jin Jiulin, Li Yaolong, Qian Yumin, Zhang Ziying, and Mao Jingen led detectives from the general task force to Chongde Fang No. 16 by car. They only found Yan's friend, Dai Yunhong, from Jiangbei. According to Dai, Yan was hiding at No. 20 Tiancheng Lane, Rue Joffre in the French Concession. The detectives then took Dai to No. 20 Tiancheng Lane, Rue Joffre, where they found Yan Er and his wife sleeping in bed. They were then arrested, along with his wife, Li, Dai, and several others, and taken to the police station. Yan confessed that he had colluded with the injured and dead people in Shanghai and Jiangbei to commit robbery, kidnapping, and extortion. This time, it was because his gang members unevenly divided the loot and were jealous of each other. At 2:00 PM that afternoon, he used the alias Wang Xizheng to rent a room at the Fasheng New Hotel and lured the four of them in to shoot them. The two people currently being treated in the hospital, Zhong Zhiqing and Jiang Yihan, i.e., Chen Yiming, and the two dead people were indeed Xia Yongsheng and the person surnamed Xue. There were also several other accomplices at large. The West Concession detective chief ordered them to be detained separately and ordered the detectives to strictly apprehend the fugitive gang members and bring them to justice for interrogation. He also praised the detectives for their rapid and diligent work in solving the case, and the detectives expressed their gratitude and left.

Cruelty of Zheng Yanzuo's Family's Wet Nurse 173

Her Nephew Was Forced to Stop Working After Being Humiliated, He Committed Suicide by Poisoning, Still Unwilling to Accept Punishment After Three Months in Custody

Zheng Yanzuo, i.e., Zheng Xiaoxu's son, lives at No. 10 Hardoon Road in Western Shanghai and employs many male and female servants. Xu Yu, a woman from Yangzhou, has been a wet nurse in the Zheng residence for many years. She is usually crude and often quarrels with other servants. Even the mistress of the house is sometimes scolded by her. In November of the previous year, Xu Yu introduced her nephew, Xu Youru (41 years old, from Yangzhou), to the Zheng residence as a shop assistant. Xu is very honest and loyal to his work and is trusted by the master. He has saved 50 yuan over the past year and stored it with Yu. Recently, because he needed to use the money, he asked Yu for it. Yu only returned 30 yuan to Xu. On the 31st of last month, Youru accidentally broke a rice bowl. Yu immediately asked the master to fire him. The master thought it was unintentional and the damage was minimal, so he only warned him. However, Yu was very dissatisfied and slapped Youru twice in the face in front of the master and forced him to leave the Zheng residence that day. She also forced the other two maids whom she had introduced to stop working at the same time, and Yu also resigned. Four days later, Youru, unable to make a living, returned to the Zheng residence and begged Yanzuo to re-employ him. Yanzuo agreed. However, Yu found out about this and rushed to the Zheng residence at about 8:00 PM on the 7th of this month. She immediately twisted and beat Youru when she saw him. The cook, Cai Jinrong, tried to dissuade her, but she left angrily and asked Youru to go to No. 985 East Yalu Road the next morning to reason with Youru's sister-in-law, Xu Yang. Therefore, at 8:00 AM on the 8th, Youru left the Zheng residence alone and went to his sister-in-law's place to meet Yu. After that, an argument broke out. In his resentment, Youru suddenly had a suicidal thought and went out to buy opium and secretly swallowed it. He returned to the Zheng residence at 11:00 AM. His colleagues saw that his face was very different and he was sweating profusely, but he said nothing. They thought he had heatstroke and quickly gave him acupuncture. At that time, Shen Yuanxiang, an old man who planted flowers in the Zheng residence, asked Xu. Xu only said the word "injustice" and nothing else. He then reported to the master, who quickly sent him to the Red Cross Hospital on Route Foch by car. However, he was too poisoned and died at about 1:00 PM in the afternoon. The hospital reported to the Jing'an Temple Police Station and ordered the body to be taken to the morgue for examination. At the same time, they ordered the arrest of Yu for further investigation. The day before yesterday afternoon, Detective Lu Gendi arrested Xu Yu and sent her to the women's detention center. The interpreter of the First Special District Court immediately asked the police station's lawyer, Qian Xunjiu, to rise and detail the above situation, saying that the police station was now prosecuting the defendant for the crime of obstructing freedom under Article 318 of the criminal law and requested that the court render a judgment in accordance with the law. Xu Youjin, the deceased's younger brother, also heard the news from his hometown and came to Shanghai to hire a lawyer to sue Xu Yu, requesting that the deceased be vindicated. Zheng Yanzuo then appeared with witnesses Shen Yuanxiang, Cai Jinrong, the deceased's sister-in-law Xu Yang, and the deceased's younger brother Xu Youjin, to testify to the above facts. When questioned, the defendant Xu Yu admitted that she had a quarrel with Youru on July 31 because he broke a bowl, but she firmly denied all other facts and hired a lawyer to defend her. After Judge Cheng Shangfeng ordered the lawyers from each side to debate, he announced in court that Xu Yu was sentenced to three months of imprisonment for the crime of using violence and coercion to obstruct the exercise of rights. The number of days of detention before the trial was allowed to be deducted from the imprisonment period at a rate of two days for one day. It is said that Xu Yu is still not satisfied with the judgment and intends to appeal.

Scandalous Affair on the Water 174

Xu Zhansan's Debauchery on a Sampan, Wang Lindi Cries and Demands the Return of Her Virginity

A local man, Gong Ziliang, makes a living by running the Rongmingyuan Teahouse at No. 107 Caofang Street, Yangjing Town, Pudong. His wife, Chen, gave birth to a son named Changsheng, who is seventeen or eighteen years old and works on a small steamship. Since childhood, through a matchmaker, he was betrothed to Wang Lindi, a girl from the nearby Shengjia Alley. Lindi, now fifteen years old, works at the Shenxin No. 9 Cotton Mill in Yangshupu, Shanghai. Every morning, she routinely takes a sampan from Yangjing Port, Pudong, to the Lan Road Wharf on the opposite bank to go to work, so she is quite familiar with the sampanmen there. On the twelfth of this month, Lindi and her neighbor Pan Quanmei (who works at the same factory) boarded Xu Zhansan's sampan, No. 1368, at Yangjing Port to cross the river. When the sampan reached the pontoon set up by the Xiangtai Lumber Company in Puxin, Xu tied the boat with a cable and suddenly had illicit relations with Lindi inside the sampan cabin (the exact time is disputed by both parties and is unknown). After the act, Xu jokingly promised to give Lindi five yuan and Quanmei three yuan within a day or two, instructing them not to make a fuss, so no one else knew about it. However, Xu is a poor man and could not come up with the eight yuan. On the fourteenth, Lindi and Quanmei met Xu at the Lan Road Wharf and demanded the money. Xu could not pay. Lindi, having lost her virginity to Xu, grabbed his clothes and cried, demanding the return of her virginity. A friend of Xu's came to mediate and advised Xu to give her five yuan first. However, Xu had no money on him. At this time, more and more people gathered to watch. A foreign police officer happened to pass by and, after learning the whole story, took all three of them to the Yangshupu Police Station. Lindi was sent to Guangren Hospital on Avenue Haig for examination. Dr. D. Sousa issued a certificate proving that Lindi's hymen had been ruptured. The police station, as the case occurred on the water, telegraphed the Water Police Station at Weituoma. Detective Sun Agui and Deng Jiagen were dispatched to bring the three back to the police station. After a preliminary interrogation by the police chief, the defendant Xu Zhansan, twenty-two years old, from Jiangbei, who rows sampan No. 1368 for a living, stated: "At about one o'clock in the afternoon on the twelfth of this month, I was repairing the awning on my boat at Yangjing Port when Wang Lindi and Pan Quanmei called me to cross the river. When we reached the middle of the river, Lindi asked me if I had a wife. I said no and that she only had a mother at home and no siblings. She voluntarily offered to marry me and pulled me to engage in illicit relations. Afterward, she asked me for five yuan to buy clothes, and Quanmei, who was keeping watch at the stern, also asked for three yuan for keeping watch. I promised to give them the money in a few days. Today, they suddenly demanded it forcefully, leading to my arrest by the foreign police. That is the truth." Wang Lindi, fifteen years old, from Pudong, a child bride in the Gong family, stated: "At four-thirty in the morning on the twelfth of this month, I took the defendant's sampan with Pan Quanmei to cross the river to go to work. Unexpectedly, the defendant stopped the boat midway and forcibly embraced me in the cabin, raping me while I screamed for help in the middle of the river. Afterward, he promised to give me five yuan and Quanmei three yuan, instructing us not to reveal the secret. But the money has not been given to this day, hence the dispute," and so on. Pan Quanmei, fourteen years old, from Pudong, gave a statement consistent with Lindi's. The police chief, noting that the times given by the two parties differed greatly, one in the afternoon and one in the morning, dispatched the original detectives to investigate. Chen San, the sampanman of No. 1329, and Chen Xiaoer, the sampanman of No. 1990, testified that Lindi and Quanmei had boarded Xu Zhansan's sampan to cross the river at one o'clock in the afternoon on the twelfth. The police chief, having completed the investigation, summoned Chen, Lindi's aunt, to the police station yesterday to take Lindi and Quanmei home temporarily. The defendant was detained in the detention center to await today's (17th) summons of witnesses to be sent to the local court for interrogation.

A Braid Costs a Life 175

Braid Caught in Machine, Severe Injury Leads to Death

Liu Guizhen, a seventeen-year-old female worker from Taizhou in the combining room of the Huafeng Cotton Mill in Wusong Yunzaobang, accidentally got her braid caught in the belt of a machine in the machine room at about four o'clock yesterday afternoon. The machine was running, and in an instant, the flesh under her hair was completely separated from her skull. Blood gushed out, a gruesome sight. Liu immediately lost consciousness. Fellow workers, upon seeing this, immediately stopped the machine and reported it to the personnel department, who urgently sent the injured person to the Haibin Public Hospital on the Outer Bund. Due to the severity of the injury and the hospital's simple equipment, they were unable to treat her and prepared a vehicle to transfer her to Shanghai Hospital for treatment. However, due to the severe injury, the rescue was ineffective, and she died at about eight o'clock in the afternoon. Her fellow townsman, Zhang Yufu, and others telegraphed her family and prepared a coffin for burial.

Seven-Story Building to be Constructed at the Intersection of Jiangxi Road and Fuzhou Road 176

Also, a Tall Tower to be Built

The Shanghai Times reports that a new building for the General Police Station and the Central Fire Brigade will soon be constructed at the southwest corner of the intersection of Jiangxi Road and Fuzhou Road. The blueprints have been completed by the Public Works Department and construction will begin in May or June. The site covers nearly six mu. It is planned to build a seven-story building along both Fuzhou and Jiangxi Roads, and a 100-foot tower will be built behind the fire brigade building. The construction cost is estimated at about one million taels and will take two years to complete.

Huangpu River Pontoons to be Improved 177

To Prevent Ships from Breaking Iron Chains

The Shanghai Times reports that an important improvement is underway in the port of this city. There are approximately eighty-four boat-mooring pontoons in the Huangpu River. Each pontoon has four anchors, each weighing seven tons, placed on the riverbed and tied down on all sides with numerous iron chains interconnected. Therefore, the total length of the iron chain used for one pontoon is no less than one thousand feet. If the water of the Huangpu River were drained, one would see a dense network of iron chains in the river, forming a long row. Recently, large ships have been entering and leaving the port in increasing numbers, and occasionally, they are pushed by the tide and break the iron chains of the pontoons. The cost of sending people into the water to repair them each year is no less than several thousand taels. Therefore, Mr. Green of the River Conservancy of the Customs Service has decided to replace them with the latest type of single-chain, single-hammer pontoons. Each pontoon will use only one giant chain, seventy-five feet long, with a giant hammer weighing eight tons attached to the bottom and buried twenty-four feet deep in the mud. The chain is as thick as a person's body, and each chain link is twenty inches long and over four inches thick, made of cast steel and rustproofed. It is purchased from the United States. The giant hammer is shaped like a square tower and is also made of cast iron by the Jiangnan Shipyard. The replacement project is currently being undertaken by the Ruirong Factory.

Public Works Bureau Relaxes Restrictions on East Xihua Road 178

The Shanghai Concession Chinese Ratepayers Association previously forwarded a letter from over a hundred businesses, including Xie Mao Xing, on East Xihua Road to the Public Works Bureau, requesting road repairs. The Association received a reply from the Public Works Bureau yesterday, stating: "In response to your letter of June 13, forwarding the letter from Xie Mao Xing and other businesses requesting the Bureau to repair East Xihua Road and pave it with asphalt to prevent dust and improve sanitation, we have investigated and found that the road is currently being planned for widening, from the original forty-foot road surface to sixty feet. Before the widening design is completed, the repair work will be temporarily delayed. Currently, the widening work is largely completed and repairs can be carried out next spring. The entire road is currently constructed of crushed stone with asphalt paving. In response to the proposal to change it to a cement road base with asphalt pavement before the repairs are carried out, we hereby reply to you."

An Amusing Incident of Japanese Mistakenly Beating Japanese 179

At 11:15 PM the night before last, at the intersection of North Sichuan Road and Shiqing Road, more than ten Japanese people carried a paper-crafted lantern boat about seven or eight feet long, inscribed with "Western Maru" in large characters, adorned with lanterns and playing gongs and drums, passing by the entrance of Shudeli Lane. Inside the lane was the China Dyeing and Finishing Company. Workers of the company were relaxing at the entrance of the lane. A worker named Hosokawa, from Nagasaki, Japan, had been in Shanghai for many years, wearing Chinese clothing, a white undershirt, and speaking Shanghainese. Because it was night, he looked like a Chinese person at first glance. As the road had not been widened and was only accessible to pedestrians, the lantern boat accidentally bumped into Hosokawa. The Japanese carrying the lantern boat mistook Hosokawa for a Chinese person and punched him. Hosokawa fought back, and they exchanged blows, resulting in a brawl. After realizing Hosokawa was also Japanese, they let go. The Shiqing Road police station, under the jurisdiction of the Fifth District, First Branch of the Public Security Bureau, upon hearing the news, dispatched Inspector Li Tingzhang and officers to mediate. The Japanese people then dispersed. After an investigation, it was learned that the previous day was the Japanese Mid-Autumn Festival, hence the lantern boat procession.

Weather Report 180

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated: hot and cloudy weather; easterly winds in the East Sea; winds in the Yellow Sea are undetermined; extremely bad weather around the Ryukyu Islands due to the storm moving north or northwest. The temperature in this city for the twenty-four hours before 3:00 PM yesterday was: highest 92.7, lowest 76.7. The highest on the same day last year was 92.7, and the lowest was 78.3.

Letter

To the esteemed editor: I am writing regarding the news item in the news column of your newspaper on the 14th, which stated that the Ningbo Native Place Association has requested the City Government to stop the forced eviction of tenants from Lianyuan Lane. This statement is inconsistent with the facts and we request it to be corrected. After investigating, we found that due to the current disorganization and inefficiency, we believe that consolidation in one location is necessary. Therefore, we decided to repossess the house at No. 3 Lianyuan Lane for our own use as an office. On June 30, we sent a registered letter to the tenant of that house, Mr. Wang Maosheng, instructing him to move out by the end of July so that we could move in. This action is in full compliance with the Shanghai housing regulations, which require one month's notice. However, Mr. Wang has delayed moving out after receiving the letter. We have repeatedly urged him to move out by the end of July, as the matter has been decided by a public resolution. To date, there has been no response. Unexpectedly, upon reading the news yesterday, it was clear that Mr. Wang Maosheng had fabricated and falsely reported the incident. In addition to investigating the facts and conducting further negotiations, we specifically request your newspaper to promptly correct this. With best wishes, Zheng Yunfang, August 16.

The Nature and Purpose of the Pacific International Studies Association by Chen Liting 181

In recent centuries, the center of gravity of international issues has gradually shifted from the Atlantic to the Pacific, a fact that has become increasingly apparent and is recognized by those who generally understand the global situation. As the Pacific is the center of gravity of international issues, the countries surrounding the Pacific and the European countries related to the Pacific have a deep relationship with it. In addition, there are many problems and hidden dangers between countries, such as the increasingly fierce economic competition and unresolved political issues. Specifically, issues such as the US-Japan immigration problem, the problem of colonial rule, and various political and economic issues between China and Japan are all sufficient to cause great disputes and hinder world peace. However, a close examination of these issues reveals that some cannot be resolved by diplomats at a moment's notice. This is because their differences are formed by the cultural situation and social thought of their countries. Therefore, if we want to seek a solution, we should first have an international organization to fully study the focus of each issue and then use it as a basis for discussion so that the facts can be clearly revealed, and an appropriate solution can be found without being limited by preconceived notions and easily leading to a breakdown. The establishment of the Pacific International Studies Association is intended to respond to the above-mentioned needs. Now, it has been established for more than six years. The main purpose is to study the conditions of various ethnic groups along the Pacific in order to promote friendship and understanding between the various ethnic groups. The first meeting was held in Honolulu in 1925. In 1927, the second meeting was held in Honolulu. In 1929, it was held in Kyoto, Japan. The number of attendees at the first meeting was relatively small. In the second and third meetings, the scale was larger, and many diplomats, scholars, and educators from various countries were recruited as members. The scope of the agenda also gradually focused on political and diplomatic aspects. The purpose and establishment process of the Pacific International Studies Association are briefly as follows.

The work of this association can be divided into three categories: (1) Research... The selection of research issues is limited to the important issues discussed at the previous meeting, where there were conflicting opinions and no factual truth to rely on. (2) Discussion (3) Publication... Based on the results of the research, a detailed discussion is then held, and then various materials are published and disseminated in the hope of creating sound public opinion to restrain preconceived notions and emotional actions. The meeting period is once every two years. The discussion method adopts a round table meeting format. Each representative is not restricted by the meeting format and can freely express their opinions. Moreover, they participate in the meeting as private individuals and are not commissioned by the government, so they can speak frankly. This is the progress of the association's work and the method of discussion. (To be continued)
