World Snippets 182

— Hai Ke

Dog Abuse Lawsuit

Hythe, England. A hotel owner had a foxhound. Short and stout. One day, he was accused of abusing the dog. He was brought to court. When the case was heard, the evidence was presented. On one hand, the dog was brought to court. The leash was removed. Unexpectedly, the dog was very happy to see its owner and pounced on him, wagging its tail and licking his face. The judge considered this a sign of affection between man and dog. The evidence of abuse was completely overturned. The dog owner was immediately released.

One-Legged Man's Bicycle

Englishman R. Baker lost a leg in the European War. Recently, while testing a newly installed prosthetic leg and a self-made bicycle that only requires the use of one leg, Rocherster rode the bicycle to Leeds, covering 226 miles in 42 hours. This one-legged general is truly dedicated.

Australia's Horses

In 1788, Australia only had five horses: one stallion, three mares, and one foal. Now, it has bred to 2.25 million horses, becoming a famous horse-producing region.

Random Chats on Maritime Countries 183

— Zizai

Ocean production is a great natural advantage. If the methods are correct, it is inexhaustible and inexhaustible. In the past, Guanzi revitalized the salt industry in Lu, leading to the prosperity of Qi. To this day, England and Japan are the leading fishing nations in the world, with annual production of over 12 million tons. Russia has 11 million tons. The United States produces less, but still 1.2 million tons. The Japanese rely heavily on fish as a staple food. More than 1.5 million people are engaged in fishing. There are over 20,000 steam fishing vessels and 380,000 ordinary fishing boats. Every year, the fish trade with China amounts to over 30 million Japanese yen. Looking back at our country, there are only six aquatic product schools. With the exception of two fishing vessels each in Guangdong and Zhejiang, the rest are old-fashioned fishing methods. The underdevelopment of aquatic products has a long history. Yesterday, I passed through Dinghai and visited the Zhejiang Vocational School of Marine Products. The marine products were extremely abundant. I was endlessly interested in the guidance and explanation of Jin Mingzhao, the principal of the school. I will describe several of them below to know the wonders of the animal kingdom of the sea.

Abalone. Originally named Fu, it belongs to the mollusk family. The shell is oval. It has feet to attach to the rocks. The shell only has one side, which is very strong. There are several holes on it. Cuttlefish is its enemy, because cuttlefish has many claws. It presses its claws on the shell holes. The air does not circulate, and the abalone suffocates and dies, and then eats its meat.

Flying fish. Only a foot long, the body is slender and round. The Zeppelin airship is modeled after its style. It has two wings on its back. It can fly out of the water for more than ten feet, but it cannot go far. There are birds on the sea that specialize in eating this fish, so it sinks. There are also enemy fish in the sea. It flies out of the sea to defend itself when encountering enemies.

Eel, commonly known as Shan. The body is long, cylindrical, and the tail is slightly flat. There is a lot of mucus. The scales are fine, and the mouth is wide. The snout is dark black, and the abdomen is white and yellow. This fish is found everywhere. But its source of growth has not yet been detected by any country in the world. If we can trace its roots and discover its source of reproduction, it will be enough to cause a sensation in the world of natural history.

Whale. It is the largest animal in the world. It looks like a fish, but it is actually a mammal. The large ones can be as long as eighty or ninety feet. They mostly live in the North Pacific. In the autumn, when the north is severely cold, they migrate south with the tide. They are found along the coast of Shandong. Its front limbs are all fin-shaped, and it has no hind limbs. The tail is flat. The nostrils are on top. It floats on the water from time to time and exhales air, which looks like a spray. Ordinary people do not observe it. Because of its large size, it is thought that it must have a large appetite. However, in fact, it is the opposite. Its throat is very narrow, less than two inches wide. Usually, it only eats plankton in the sea. It cannot swallow fish larger than a foot.

Other things, such as where there are sea coconuts, there are sea corals. Jiang Yaozhu belongs to the shellfish family, not the fish family. There is also a kind of fighting fish, which is bright and lovely. It is known that besides cockfighting and bullfighting, there is also fighting fish. At present, our country is paying little attention to it. In European and American countries, it has long become a gambling game.

Coffee Musings 184

— Yanyu

Coffee is a tropical plant. It is mainly produced in Africa, followed by South America. It needs to be refined before it can be used as a beverage. In the early days, only tropical natives liked to drink it. Later, as overseas trade flourished, it spread all over the world. As for today, the trend of drinking coffee has become widespread among all races in the world. Those who like it often become addicted to it, just like smoking and drinking. Now, I have collected some interesting anecdotes about coffee from overseas and woven them into this article for your reading pleasure.

African natives are addicted to it. African natives have been drinking coffee for the longest time. It has been more than 600 years of history. It was invented in the early 14th century. Although the way of drinking has undergone countless reforms, the natives' addiction has never changed. Africa is located in the tropics, where it is hot all year round, and noon is especially unbearable. Therefore, the natives are mostly lazy. They like to lie naked in the shade of palm trees to spend the day. They only get up in the evening. Then they gather to sing and dance under the moonlight and starlight, and drink coffee to their heart's content. With a cup in hand, they forget everything. They have the air of not being inferior to a king facing south.

Popular in London, England, very early. England was in the 16th century, when Queen Elizabeth was in power. She actively developed overseas trade and opened the way for today's imperial colonies. At that time, coffee and tea began to be imported from Africa and China. However, the quantity was small, and few people drank them. However, it was popular among the royal nobles of London as a rare drink. There is also a small anecdote in between, which is still passed on as a topic of conversation among the British people. Queen Elizabeth loved literature and promoted it wholeheartedly. At that time, the great playwright Shakespeare was especially favored. One day, he was summoned to the inner court. Because his answers were satisfactory, he was specially rewarded with a cup of the finest coffee for royal use. Shakespeare, overwhelmed by the honor, drank it all in one gulp. After a while, he tasted the strange bitterness. He frowned and said nothing. The Queen, seeing this, could not help but smile. This was the first time Shakespeare had drunk coffee.

Coffee shops all over Baghdad. Arabs are naturally fond of listening to stories, and the habit of drinking coffee is also popular. Baghdad, the capital of Iraq, is a magnificent city full of oriental flavor. If we travel to that place, we can see that there are many coffee shops on the streets and in the markets. According to a survey by the Englishman Wilbur in the summer of 1930, there were as many as 250 coffee shops of all sizes in Baghdad. If you go to each coffee shop, you will always find an old Arab or Turk sitting high on a couch, telling stories to the audience. The fragrant aroma of coffee and tobacco fills the room. The people of the subjugated country are drunk. After sighing, they use coffee and tobacco to relieve their depression. This scene is truly poetic.

Washington Irving's great addiction. The late American writer Washington Irving was a prolific writer and well-known for his writing. He loved to travel throughout his life, especially to visit historical sites. He traveled all over Europe, especially lingering in Spain. In his later years, he was appointed by the US government as the Minister to Spain. Therefore, he had deep feelings for the Spanish people. According to Spanish folk legends, Irving was addicted to coffee throughout his life. After living in Spain, he became more assimilated by the local people. The Spanish people's addiction to coffee is far greater than that of the Americans. Ordinary people drink coffee after meals at a certain time. But Irving needs to drink it when he wakes up in the morning. Coffee accounts for almost nine-tenths of his drinks all day long. Whenever he is writing, the coffee pot is indispensable. Otherwise, his thoughts will become slow.

The Admirable Old Ways of Wei Ruosou 185

— Zhang

Wei Ruosou, an old gentleman from Hengyang, is over seventy years old. He has devoted himself to the six arts, and his calligraphy and painting are profound and not outdated. He had a close friendship with his late teacher, Zeng Nongran, and obtained something that had never been seen before. Last winter, Mr. Zeng and Ruosou were about to hold a birthday banquet together for their 70th birthdays. However, Mr. Zeng suddenly passed away before his birthday. Ruosou was deeply saddened. The toast was immediately interrupted. Remembering that when Mr. Zeng was seriously ill, he wrote a small landscape painting for Ruosou, with a poem inscribed on it: "The Juexi River flows around the pavilion, and the hand-planted garden willows have become embankments. After the calamity, there is still my humble house. I regret that I have not been able to return every year." This painting was Mr. Zeng's last work, which shows the deep friendship between the two old gentlemen. Recently, Mr. Wu Jianqiu sent a collection of poems from Beijing to celebrate Ruosou's birthday, as well as a postscript poem: "I grew up with you during the Xuanhe period, and we are truly like old men who have silenced their zithers. I cannot believe that time flies by like a rolling wheel. It is pitiful that my ambition still depends on the mausoleum. The horizontal forest is worm-eaten, and there is no complete leaf. After being drunk, the dragons and snakes are all over the reed mat. My teachers and friends are withered and I am old. No one understands my heart at this time. I often say that life is rare at seventy. I am happy to rest from the dust. Hearing too much only adds to the burden of my body. Warmth and fullness have always been contrary to the Tao. I look at the remaining ink stains in the inkstone. Whose well is white, reflecting the thorn door? Is there anything else you know? The lonely crane will return three thousand years later." Mr. Ruosou's 70th birthday was on the seventh day of the eleventh lunar month in the year of Gengwu. Mr. and his forgotten friend Nongran passed away one day apart. Mr. Nongran unfortunately passed away several months ago. Mr. is saddened by the passing of his peers and stopped the birthday toast. His noble heart and ancient friendship are deeply admirable. I collected two poems by Lu Jiannan, which are not very well written, to express my congratulations from afar. Wu Yi wrote the book in the middle of the summer in the year of Xinwei. His poems are lofty and soaring, truly worthy of being passed down. It also shows that the friendship between Mr. Zeng, Ruosou, and Jian is not easily changed by life and death. When I was fifty years old last month, I was honored by the presence of Ruosou, who was old and had white hair. He was energetic and had a moving demeanor. His language was witty and meaningful. This autumn, on July 4, it will be the anniversary of Mr. Zeng's death. Ruosou also wants to participate in the memorial meeting of the Zeng-Li same-sect association. His ancient sentiments and noble friendship do not change even in life and death. Ruosou can truly correct the bad customs and superficial habits of the late period. (Instead of Repaying)

Correction: In the "Elegy for Xu Qishang, a man of the same year" published yesterday, the phrase "diao zhi" (to mourn him) in the seventh line of the poem was mistakenly placed on the ninth line and should be corrected immediately.

Travels in India (83) 186

— Linghua

The Sana University has not yet opened. Outside its gate, under a tree, there is a free elementary school with a blackboard. A flat platform is made of cement. Under the big tree, there are more than ten children learning to read and do arithmetic. This is the Indian rural elementary school. The clothes of all the children in the class are not worth one yuan. The life is quite similar to the elementary schools I saw in Myanmar and Hungary. Walking between two trees, I saw two teachers teaching two classes of elementary school students. Each class has about twenty students. There are no desks, benches, or houses. Just two big trees, which can be called the Twin Tree School. Because Buddha Nirvana was also at the twin trees. The children each hold a pen and have a slate to sit on the ground. A sack is laid on the ground. Indian rural schools for common people are so simple. However, I also often visit various royal residences. Their arrangements are luxurious and definitely not inferior to Westerners. The harm of the class system is extreme. I visit the homes of wealthy people in major cities, and their arrangements are all exquisite. Every meal is like a Western meal at a Western restaurant in Shanghai. How poor the countryside is! Alas, I often see life on small broken boats on various rivers. I wonder what God is. Why did He create this Earth with uneven heat and cold, dangerous mountains and rivers, and unequal races? If not for Marx's grand vision, how can we make them all equal? It is truly not easy to say.

Indians' gambling seems not as serious as the Chinese. Their gambling tools are also different. In the park, I saw several Indians playing cards. The police came to watch, but did not interfere.

The village system in India: a village has a village chief, called Mukhi. Six or seven villages form a township, with a chief called Choki. The Choki has policemen subordinate to him. Six or seven Chokis form a town, with a Thana (police station). Ten or eleven towns form a TahsiI. Four or five TahsiIs form a county. The head of a county is about one hundred English miles long and fifty English miles wide. Below the county, there is a four-level system, also known as cities, towns, townships, and villages. Five or six counties form a Division. Four or five Divisions form a province. Provinces are either large or small. Indian village houses are quite solid, not as makeshift as those of the Burmese. Compared to the Burmese, Indians are like thousand-year-old pines and cypresses, with dragon scales bristling. The Burmese are like willows, with drooping branches that are charming and lovely.

Rotary Club Speech

Women, Women (22) 187

— Yao Sufeng

"Miss! The person who came downstairs is really strange!" As soon as Qiu Zi saw Miss Ding, she hesitated and felt it was difficult to say it directly.

"What's so strange? Tell me!" Miss Ding laughed.

"It's a woman who came, she said she is Mr. Lu's..." Qiu Zi said halfway, then couldn't finish.

"Why can't you say it clearly and straightforwardly? Mr. Lu's what?" Miss Ding also became suspicious.

Qiu Zi had no choice but to say, "The woman who came, she said she is Mr. Lu's wife...

She came to find her husband!"

Before she finished speaking, Miss Ding suffered a major blow to her nerves. All her emotions were in chaotic turmoil, and finally she became somewhat dazed. Suddenly, she jumped up from the sofa and said loudly, "Is there such a thing?"

When Qiu Zi saw that the Miss's expression was not right, she knew that this matter was going to cause a big stir. But she had absolutely no way to comfort her Miss, she only said, "That's what the woman said, but maybe there are other reasons inside!"

"Is that woman still downstairs? Go and invite her in, I'll ask her myself to find out what's going on!" Miss Ding said calmly, but her hands and feet were somewhat trembling. She followed Qiu Zi downstairs, and Qiu Zi went to invite Xiao Rong's wife inside.

Like a flower, Miss Ding was found in Xiao Rong's wife's eyes. She still seemed to remember the scene of buying gardenias from her at the Suzhou train station. But she couldn't get angry, even though she thought the Miss Ding standing opposite her was the enemy who took away her husband.

Miss Ding asked with a trembling voice, "Are you Mr. Lu's wife?... Alas! Poor thing!... Why didn't I know sooner?" Miss Ding shed tears.

Xiao Rong's wife felt very strange. Originally, women's tears are most likely to move people's emotions. Seeing Miss Ding cry, she felt even more indecisive, and just stared blankly at Miss Ding in a daze. After all, she also began to cry.

Qiu Zi brought tea in. When she saw that both of them were wiping their tears, she was also puzzled. She could only try her best to persuade Miss Ding, saying, "It's good to say things clearly. It's not worth it to make yourself sick!"

Miss Ding then reluctantly suppressed the sorrow in her heart and talked to Xiao Rong's wife in detail. Xiao Rong's wife then felt that Miss Ding was also a very good woman, but she was deceived by her husband, so she also suffered because of her husband. Therefore, she not only did not hate Miss Ding, but instead felt sympathy for Miss Ding.

The Yanzhe Hospital on Xinqiao Street announced that this hospital was founded by Mr. Zhao Yanzhe, a medical graduate from Japan. Recently, because the original hospital site was insufficient, a second hospital was established on Zilaihuo Street. The director is his nephew, Mr. Zhao Zhemin. An obstetrics department has been added, and four specialist female obstetricians have been hired. Deliveries have now begun, etc.

The Zhu Jichang Pharmacy in Hongqingfang, North Sichuan Road, announced that this pharmacy has invented a "Wan Ying Green Medicine Water," a medicine that is pure and mild, and can be taken internally or applied externally. It is effective for treating acute and chronic childhood convulsions, summer heatstroke, vomiting, diarrhea, rheumatism, bruises, etc. Free samples are now being offered, but no money will be charged. Sorry, no postal service is available, etc.
